##### **Beyond Functional Correctness: Design Issues in AI IDE-Generated Large-Scale Projects**
2604.06373v1 by Syed Mohammad Kashif, Ruiyin Li, Peng Liang, Amjed Tahir, Qiong Feng, Zengyang Li, Mojtaba Shahin

New generation of AI coding tools, including AI-powered IDEs equipped with agentic capabilities, can generate code within the context of the project. These AI IDEs are increasingly perceived as capable of producing project-level code at scale. However, there is limited empirical evidence on the extent to which they can generate large-scale software systems and what design issues such systems may exhibit. To address this gap, we conducted a study to explore the capability of Cursor in generating large-scale projects and to evaluate the design quality of projects generated by Cursor. First, we propose a Feature-Driven Human-In-The-Loop (FD-HITL) framework that systematically guides project generation from curated project descriptions. We generated 10 projects using Cursor with the FD-HITL framework across three application domains and multiple technologies. We assessed the functional correctness of these projects through manual evaluation, obtaining an average functional correctness score of 91%. Next, we analyzed the generated projects using two static analysis tools, CodeScene and SonarQube, to detect design issues. We identified 1,305 design issues categorized into 9 categories by CodeScene and 3,193 issues in 11 categories by SonarQube. Our findings show that (1) when used with the FD-HITL framework, Cursor can generate functional large-scale projects averaging 16,965 LoC and 114 files; (2) the generated projects nevertheless contain design issues that may pose long-term maintainability and evolvability risks, requiring careful review by experienced developers; (3) the most prevalent issues include Code Duplication, high Code Complexity, Large Methods, Framework Best-Practice Violations, Exception-Handling Issues and Accessibility Issues; (4) these design issues violate design principles such as SRP, SoC, and DRY. The replication package is at https://github.com/Kashifraz/DIinAGP

摘要：新一代的 AI 編碼工具，包括具備代理能力的 AI 驅動 IDE，可以在項目的上下文中生成代碼。這些 AI IDE 越來越被認為能夠大規模地生成項目級代碼。然而，關於它們能生成大規模軟體系統的程度以及這些系統可能出現的設計問題，實證證據有限。為了填補這一空白，我們進行了一項研究，以探討 Cursor 在生成大規模項目方面的能力，並評估 Cursor 生成的項目的設計質量。首先，我們提出了一個以特徵驅動的人機協作（FD-HITL）框架，系統性地指導從策劃的項目描述中生成項目。我們使用 FD-HITL 框架通過 Cursor 生成了 10 個項目，涵蓋三個應用領域和多種技術。我們通過手動評估這些項目的功能正確性，獲得了平均功能正確性分數為 91%。接下來，我們使用兩個靜態分析工具 CodeScene 和 SonarQube 來分析生成的項目，以檢測設計問題。我們在 CodeScene 中識別了 1,305 個設計問題，分為 9 類，而在 SonarQube 中識別了 3,193 個問題，分為 11 類。我們的研究結果顯示：(1) 當與 FD-HITL 框架一起使用時，Cursor 可以生成平均 16,965 行代碼和 114 個文件的功能性大規模項目；(2) 生成的項目仍然包含可能對長期可維護性和可演進性造成風險的設計問題，需要經驗豐富的開發者仔細審查；(3) 最常見的問題包括代碼重複、高代碼複雜性、大方法、框架最佳實踐違規、異常處理問題和可訪問性問題；(4) 這些設計問題違反了如單一職責原則（SRP）、分離關注（SoC）和不重複自己（DRY）等設計原則。複製包位於 https://github.com/Kashifraz/DIinAGP

##### **LAG-XAI: A Lie-Inspired Affine Geometric Framework for Interpretable Paraphrasing in Transformer Latent Spaces**
2604.06086v1 by Olexander Mazurets, Olexander Barmak, Leonid Bedratyuk, Iurii Krak

Modern Transformer-based language models achieve strong performance in natural language processing tasks, yet their latent semantic spaces remain largely uninterpretable black boxes. This paper introduces LAG-XAI (Lie Affine Geometry for Explainable AI), a novel geometric framework that models paraphrasing not as discrete word substitutions, but as a structured affine transformation within the embedding space. By conceptualizing paraphrasing as a continuous geometric flow on a semantic manifold, we propose a computationally efficient mean-field approximation, inspired by local Lie group actions. This allows us to decompose paraphrase transitions into geometrically interpretable components: rotation, deformation, and translation. Experiments on the noisy PIT-2015 Twitter corpus, encoded with Sentence-BERT, reveal a "linear transparency" phenomenon. The proposed affine operator achieves an AUC of 0.7713. By normalizing against random chance (AUC 0.5), the model captures approximately 80% of the non-linear baseline's effective classification capacity (AUC 0.8405), offering explicit parametric interpretability in exchange for a marginal drop in absolute accuracy. The model identifies fundamental geometric invariants, including a stable matrix reconfiguration angle (~27.84°) and near-zero deformation, indicating local isometry. Cross-domain generalization is confirmed via direct cross-corpus validation on an independent TURL dataset. Furthermore, the practical utility of LAG-XAI is demonstrated in LLM hallucination detection: using a "cheap geometric check," the model automatically detected 95.3% of factual distortions on the HaluEval dataset by registering deviations beyond the permissible semantic corridor. This approach provides a mathematically grounded, resource-efficient path toward the mechanistic interpretability of Transformers.

摘要：現代基於Transformer的語言模型在自然語言處理任務中表現優異，但它們的潛在語義空間仍然大多是不可解釋的黑箱。本文介紹了LAG-XAI（可解釋人工智慧的李仿射幾何），這是一個新穎的幾何框架，將意義重述建模為嵌入空間中的結構性仿射變換，而非離散的單詞替換。通過將意義重述概念化為語義流形上的連續幾何流，我們提出了一種計算上高效的均場近似，靈感來自於局部李群作用。這使我們能夠將意義重述的轉變分解為幾何可解釋的組件：旋轉、變形和位移。在用Sentence-BERT編碼的噪聲PIT-2015 Twitter語料庫上的實驗顯示出一種「線性透明性」現象。所提出的仿射運算符達到了0.7713的AUC。通過與隨機機會（AUC 0.5）進行標準化，該模型捕捉了約80%的非線性基線的有效分類能力（AUC 0.8405），以明確的參數可解釋性換取了絕對準確性的輕微下降。該模型識別出基本的幾何不變量，包括穩定的矩陣重配置角度（約27.84°）和接近零的變形，顯示出局部等距性。通過在獨立的TURL數據集上進行直接的跨語料庫驗證，確認了跨領域的泛化。此外，LAG-XAI在LLM幻覺檢測中的實際效用得到了證明：通過使用「廉價的幾何檢查」，該模型自動檢測了HaluEval數據集上95.3%的事實扭曲，通過註冊超出允許語義範圍的偏差。這種方法提供了一條數學上有根據、資源高效的路徑，朝向Transformer的機械可解釋性。

##### **Harnessing Hyperbolic Geometry for Harmful Prompt Detection and Sanitization**
2604.06285v1 by Igor Maljkovic, Maria Rosaria Briglia, Iacopo Masi, Antonio Emanuele Cinà, Fabio Roli

Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have become essential for tasks such as image synthesis, captioning, and retrieval by aligning textual and visual information in a shared embedding space. Yet, this flexibility also makes them vulnerable to malicious prompts designed to produce unsafe content, raising critical safety concerns. Existing defenses either rely on blacklist filters, which are easily circumvented, or on heavy classifier-based systems, both of which are costly and fragile under embedding-level attacks. We address these challenges with two complementary components: Hyperbolic Prompt Espial (HyPE) and Hyperbolic Prompt Sanitization (HyPS). HyPE is a lightweight anomaly detector that leverages the structured geometry of hyperbolic space to model benign prompts and detect harmful ones as outliers. HyPS builds on this detection by applying explainable attribution methods to identify and selectively modify harmful words, neutralizing unsafe intent while preserving the original semantics of user prompts. Through extensive experiments across multiple datasets and adversarial scenarios, we prove that our framework consistently outperforms prior defenses in both detection accuracy and robustness. Together, HyPE and HyPS offer an efficient, interpretable, and resilient approach to safeguarding VLMs against malicious prompt misuse.

摘要：視覺-語言模型（VLMs）已成為圖像合成、標題生成和檢索等任務的關鍵，通過在共享嵌入空間中對齊文本和視覺信息。然而，這種靈活性也使它們容易受到旨在生成不安全內容的惡意提示的攻擊，從而引發了重要的安全擔憂。現有的防禦措施要麼依賴於黑名單過濾器，這些過濾器容易被繞過，要麼依賴於重型分類器系統，這兩者在嵌入層級攻擊下都是昂貴且脆弱的。我們通過兩個互補的組件來解決這些挑戰：超曲率提示監測（HyPE）和超曲率提示清洗（HyPS）。HyPE是一種輕量級的異常檢測器，利用超曲率空間的結構幾何來建模良性提示並將有害提示檢測為異常值。HyPS基於這一檢測，應用可解釋的歸因方法來識別和選擇性地修改有害詞彙，消除不安全的意圖，同時保留用戶提示的原始語義。通過在多個數據集和對抗場景中的廣泛實驗，我們證明了我們的框架在檢測準確性和穩健性方面始終優於先前的防禦措施。總體而言，HyPE和HyPS提供了一種高效、可解釋且具有韌性的方式，以保護VLMs免受惡意提示濫用的影響。

##### **DosimeTron: Automating Personalized Monte Carlo Radiation Dosimetry in PET/CT with Agentic AI**
2604.06280v1 by Eleftherios Tzanis, Michail E. Klontzas, Antonios Tzortzakakis

Purpose: To develop and evaluate DosimeTron, an agentic AI system for automated patient-specific MC internal radiation dosimetry in PET/CT examinations.
  Materials and Methods: In this retrospective study, DosimeTron was evaluated on a publicly available PSMA-PET/CT dataset comprising 597 studies from 378 male patients acquired on three scanner models (18-F, n = 369; 68-Ga, n = 228). The system uses GPT-5.2 as its reasoning engine and 23 tools exposed via four Model Context Protocol servers, automating DICOM metadata extraction, image preprocessing, MC simulation, organ segmentation, and dosimetric reporting through natural-language interaction. Agentic performance was assessed using diverse prompt templates spanning single-turn instructions of varying specificity and multi-turn conversational exchanges, monitored via OpenTelemetry traces. Dosimetric accuracy was validated against OpenDose3D across 114 cases and 22 organs using Pearson's r, Lin's concordance correlation coefficient (CCC), and Bland-Altman analysis.
  Results: Across all prompt templates and all runs, no execution failures, pipeline errors, or hallucinated outputs were observed. Pearson's r ranged from 0.965 to 1.000 (median 0.997; all p < 0.001) and CCC from 0.963 to 1.000 (median 0.996). Mean absolute percentage difference was below 5% for 19 of 22 organs (median 2.5%). Total per-study processing time (SD) was 32.3 (6.0) minutes.
  Conclusion: DosimeTron autonomously executed complex dosimetry pipelines across diverse prompt configurations and achieved high dosimetric agreement with OpenDose3D at clinically acceptable processing times, demonstrating the feasibility of agentic AI for patient-specific Monte Carlo dosimetry in PET/CT.

摘要：目的：開發和評估DosimeTron，一個用於PET/CT檢查中自動化患者特定MC內部輻射劑量計算的代理AI系統。<lb/>  
材料與方法：在這項回顧性研究中，評估了DosimeTron在一個公開可用的PSMA-PET/CT數據集中，該數據集包含來自378名男性患者的597項研究，這些研究是在三種掃描儀模型上獲得的（18-F，n = 369；68-Ga，n = 228）。該系統使用GPT-5.2作為其推理引擎，並通過四個模型上下文協議伺服器暴露23個工具，自動化DICOM元數據提取、圖像預處理、MC模擬、器官分割和劑量報告，通過自然語言交互進行。代理性能使用多樣的提示模板進行評估，這些模板涵蓋了不同特異性的單回合指令和多回合對話交流，通過OpenTelemetry跟踪進行監控。劑量準確性在114個案例和22個器官中使用Pearson's r、Lin的一致性相關係數（CCC）和Bland-Altman分析進行驗證。<lb/>  
結果：在所有提示模板和所有運行中，未觀察到執行失敗、管道錯誤或幻覺輸出。Pearson's r範圍從0.965到1.000（中位數0.997；所有p < 0.001），CCC範圍從0.963到1.000（中位數0.996）。22個器官中有19個的平均絕對百分比差異低於5%（中位數2.5%）。每項研究的總處理時間（標準差）為32.3（6.0）分鐘。<lb/>  
結論：DosimeTron在多樣的提示配置中自主執行複雜的劑量計算管道，並在臨床可接受的處理時間內與OpenDose3D達成高劑量一致性，顯示了代理AI在PET/CT中進行患者特定蒙特卡羅劑量計算的可行性。

##### **Analogical Reasoning as a Doctor: A Foundation Model for Gastrointestinal Endoscopy Diagnosis**
2604.05649v1 by Peixi Peng, Housheng Xie, Yanling Wei, Guangcong Ruan, Xiaoyang Zou, Qian Cao, Yongjian Nian, Guoyan Zheng

Gastrointestinal diseases impose a growing global health burden, and endoscopy is a primary tool for early diagnosis. However, routine endoscopic image interpretation still suffers from missed lesions and limited efficiency. Although AI-assisted diagnosis has shown promise, existing models often lack generalizability, adaptability, robustness, and scalability because of limited medical data, domain shift, and heterogeneous annotations. To address these challenges, we develop RATNet, a foundation model for gastrointestinal endoscopy imaging based on analogical reasoning. RATNet acquires and transfers knowledge from heterogeneous expert annotations across five gastrointestinal endoscopy datasets through a cyclic pre-training strategy. Its architecture consists of an encoder, a relevance-knowledge acquisition and transfer (RAT) module, a projector, and a multi-task head, and supports fine-tuning, linear probing, and zero-shot transfer. Evaluations show that RATNet outperforms existing foundation models, including GastroNet and GastroVision, across six scenarios: diagnosis of common gastrointestinal diseases, few-shot learning for rare diseases, zero-shot transfer to new medical sites, robustness under long-tailed disease distributions, adaptation to novel diseases, and privacy-preserving deployment via federated learning. Its advantage comes from an analogical reasoning mechanism that matches image-derived posterior knowledge to a learned prior knowledge base and transfers relative knowledge to guide diagnosis, improving generalization and resistance to bias. RATNet is open and cost-effective, supports automatic integration of heterogeneous annotations without manual label unification, and reduces data acquisition costs, making it a practical foundation for intelligent gastrointestinal diagnosis, especially in resource-limited settings.

摘要：腸胃疾病對全球健康造成日益增長的負擔，而內視鏡檢查是早期診斷的主要工具。<lb/>然而，常規的內視鏡影像解讀仍然面臨漏診和效率有限的問題。<lb/>儘管AI輔助診斷顯示出潛力，但現有模型往往缺乏普遍性、適應性、穩健性和可擴展性，原因在於醫療數據有限、領域轉移和異質標註。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們開發了RATNet，一個基於類比推理的腸胃內視鏡影像基礎模型。<lb/>RATNet通過循環預訓練策略從五個腸胃內視鏡數據集中獲取並轉移來自異質專家標註的知識。<lb/>其架構由編碼器、相關知識獲取與轉移（RAT）模塊、投影器和多任務頭組成，並支持微調、線性探測和零樣本轉移。<lb/>評估顯示，RATNet在六個場景中超越了現有的基礎模型，包括GastroNet和GastroVision：常見腸胃疾病的診斷、稀有疾病的少樣本學習、新醫療場地的零樣本轉移、在長尾疾病分佈下的穩健性、對新疾病的適應，以及通過聯邦學習實現的隱私保護部署。<lb/>其優勢來自於一種類比推理機制，該機制將影像衍生的後驗知識與學習的先驗知識庫相匹配，並轉移相對知識以指導診斷，從而提高了泛化能力和抗偏見能力。<lb/>RATNet是開放且具成本效益的，支持自動整合異質標註而無需手動標籤統一，並降低數據獲取成本，使其成為智能腸胃診斷的實用基礎，特別是在資源有限的環境中。

##### **INTERACT: An AI-Driven Extended Reality Framework for Accesible Communication Featuring Real-Time Sign Language Interpretation and Emotion Recognition**
2604.05605v1 by Nikolaos D. Tantaroudas, Andrew J. McCracken, Ilias Karachalios, Evangelos Papatheou

Video conferencing has become central to professional collaboration, yet most platforms offer limited support for deaf, hard-of-hearing, and multilingual users. The World Health Organisation estimates that over 430 million people worldwide require rehabilitation for disabling hearing loss, a figure projected to exceed 700 million by 2050. Conventional accessibility measures remain constrained by high costs, limited availability, and logistical barriers, while Extended Reality (XR) technologies open new possibilities for immersive and inclusive communication. This paper presents INTERACT (Inclusive Networking for Translation and Embodied Real-Time Augmented Communication Tool), an AI-driven XR platform that integrates real-time speech-to-text conversion, International Sign Language (ISL) rendering through 3D avatars, multilingual translation, and emotion recognition within an immersive virtual environment. Built on the CORTEX2 framework and deployed on Meta Quest 3 headsets, INTERACT combines Whisper for speech recognition, NLLB for multilingual translation, RoBERTa for emotion classification, and Google MediaPipe for gesture extraction. Pilot evaluations were conducted in two phases, first with technical experts from academia and industry, and subsequently with members of the deaf community. The trials reported 92% user satisfaction, transcription accuracy above 85%, and 90% emotion-detection precision, with a mean overall experience rating of 4.6 out of 5.0 and 90% of participants willing to take part in further testing. The results highlight strong potential for advancing accessibility across educational, cultural, and professional settings. An extended version of this work, including full pilot data and implementation details, has been published as an Open Research Europe article [Tantaroudas et al., 2026a].

摘要：視訊會議已成為專業協作的核心，但大多數平台對於聽障、重聽和多語言使用者的支援有限。世界衛生組織估計，全球有超過4.3億人需要因殘疾性聽力損失而進行康復，這一數字預計到2050年將超過7億。傳統的無障礙措施受到高成本、有限可用性和後勤障礙的限制，而擴增實境（XR）技術則為沉浸式和包容性溝通開辟了新可能。本文介紹了INTERACT（包容性翻譯和具身實時增強溝通工具），這是一個基於AI的XR平台，整合了實時語音轉文字、通用手語（ISL）透過3D虛擬角色的呈現、多語言翻譯和情感識別，並在沉浸式虛擬環境中運行。INTERACT基於CORTEX2框架，並在Meta Quest 3頭戴式顯示器上部署，結合了Whisper進行語音識別、NLLB進行多語言翻譯、RoBERTa進行情感分類，以及Google MediaPipe進行手勢提取。試點評估分兩個階段進行，首先與來自學術界和行業的技術專家進行，隨後與聽障社群成員進行。試驗報告顯示92%的用戶滿意度，轉錄準確率超過85%，情感檢測精確度為90%，整體體驗平均評分為4.6（滿分5.0），90%的參與者願意參加進一步的測試。結果突顯了在教育、文化和專業環境中推進無障礙的強大潛力。這項工作的擴展版本，包括完整的試點數據和實施細節，已作為Open Research Europe文章發表[Tantaroudas et al., 2026a]。

##### **ResearchEVO: An End-to-End Framework for Automated Scientific Discovery and Documentation**
2604.05587v1 by Zhe Zhao, Haibin Wen, Jiaming Ma, Jiachang Zhan, Tianyi Xu, Ye Wei, Qingfu Zhang

An important recurring pattern in scientific breakthroughs is a two-stage process: an initial phase of undirected experimentation that yields an unexpected finding, followed by a retrospective phase that explains why the finding works and situates it within existing theory. We present ResearchEVO, an end-to-end framework that computationally instantiates this discover-then-explain paradigm. The Evolution Phase employs LLM-guided bi-dimensional co-evolution -- simultaneously optimizing both algorithmic logic and overall architecture -- to search the space of code implementations purely by fitness, without requiring any understanding of the solutions it produces. The Writing Phase then takes the best-performing algorithm and autonomously generates a complete, publication-ready research paper through sentence-level retrieval-augmented generation with explicit anti-hallucination verification and automated experiment design. To our knowledge, ResearchEVO is the first system to cover this full pipeline end to end: no prior work jointly performs principled algorithm evolution and literature-grounded scientific documentation. We validate the framework on two cross-disciplinary scientific problems -- Quantum Error Correction using real Google quantum hardware data, and Physics-Informed Neural Networks -- where the Evolution Phase discovered human-interpretable algorithmic mechanisms that had not been previously proposed in the respective domain literatures. In both cases, the Writing Phase autonomously produced compilable LaTeX manuscripts that correctly grounded these blind discoveries in existing theory via RAG, with zero fabricated citations.

摘要：一個在科學突破中重要的重複模式是兩階段過程：初始階段的無指導實驗產生意想不到的發現，隨後是回顧階段解釋為何該發現有效並將其置於現有理論中。我們提出了ResearchEVO，一個端到端的框架，計算上實現了這一發現-然後-解釋的範式。演化階段採用LLM指導的雙維共同演化——同時優化算法邏輯和整體架構——來純粹通過適應度搜索代碼實現的空間，而不需要理解其產生的解決方案。然後，寫作階段採取表現最佳的算法，自動生成一篇完整的、準備發表的研究論文，通過句子級檢索增強生成，並進行明確的反幻覺驗證和自動實驗設計。據我們所知，ResearchEVO是第一個涵蓋這整個端到端流程的系統：沒有先前的工作同時執行原則性的算法演化和基於文獻的科學文檔。我們在兩個跨學科的科學問題上驗證了該框架——使用真實的Google量子硬體數據的量子錯誤修正，以及物理知識驅動的神經網絡——在這些情況下，演化階段發現了在各自領域文獻中未曾提出的人類可解釋的算法機制。在這兩種情況下，寫作階段自動生成了可編譯的LaTeX手稿，通過RAG正確地將這些盲目發現置於現有理論中，且沒有虛構的引用。

##### **From Large Language Model Predicates to Logic Tensor Networks: Neurosymbolic Offer Validation in Regulated Procurement**
2604.05539v1 by Cedric Haufe, Frieder Stolzenburg

We present a neurosymbolic approach, i.e., combining symbolic and subsymbolic artificial intelligence, to validating offer documents in regulated public institutions. We employ a language model to extract information and then aggregate with an LTN (Logic Tensor Network) to make an auditable decision. In regulated public institutions, decisions must be made in a manner that is both factually correct and legally verifiable. Our neurosymbolic approach allows existing domain-specific knowledge to be linked to the semantic text understanding of language models. The decisions resulting from our pipeline can be justified by predicate values, rule truth values, and corresponding text passages, which enables rule checking based on a real corpus of offer documents. Our experiments on a real corpus show that the proposed pipeline achieves performance comparable to existing models, while its key advantage lies in its interpretability, modular predicate extraction, and explicit support for XAI (Explainable AI).

摘要：我們提出了一種神經符號方法，即結合符號和亞符號人工智慧，以驗證受監管公共機構的報價文件。我們使用語言模型來提取信息，然後與 LTN（邏輯張量網絡）進行聚合，以做出可審計的決策。在受監管的公共機構中，決策必須以事實正確且法律可驗證的方式進行。我們的神經符號方法允許將現有的特定領域知識與語言模型的語義文本理解相連接。我們的流程所產生的決策可以通過謂詞值、規則真值和相應的文本段落來進行辯護，這使得基於真實的報價文件語料庫進行規則檢查成為可能。我們在真實語料庫上的實驗顯示，所提出的流程達到了與現有模型相當的性能，而其主要優勢在於可解釋性、模塊化謂詞提取以及對 XAI（可解釋人工智慧）的明確支持。

##### **Auditable Agents**
2604.05485v1 by Yi Nian, Aojie Yuan, Haiyue Zhang, Jiate Li, Yue Zhao

LLM agents call tools, query databases, delegate tasks, and trigger external side effects. Once an agent system can act in the world, the question is no longer only whether harmful actions can be prevented--it is whether those actions remain answerable after deployment. We distinguish accountability (the ability to determine compliance and assign responsibility), auditability (the system property that makes accountability possible), and auditing (the process of reconstructing behavior from trustworthy evidence). Our claim is direct: no agent system can be accountable without auditability.
  To make this operational, we define five dimensions of agent auditability, i.e., action recoverability, lifecycle coverage, policy checkability, responsibility attribution, and evidence integrity, and identify three mechanism classes (detect, enforce, recover) whose temporal information-and-intervention constraints explain why, in practice, no single approach suffices. We support the position with layered evidence rather than a single benchmark: lower-bound ecosystem measurements suggest that even basic security prerequisites for auditability are widely unmet (617 security findings across six prominent open-source projects); runtime feasibility results show that pre-execution mediation with tamper-evident records adds only 8.3 ms median overhead; and controlled recovery experiments show that responsibility-relevant information can be partially recovered even when conventional logs are missing. We propose an Auditability Card for agent systems and identify six open research problems organized by mechanism class.

摘要：LLM 代理呼叫工具、查詢資料庫、委派任務並觸發外部副作用。<lb/>一旦代理系統能夠在世界中行動，問題不再僅僅是是否能防止有害行為——而是這些行為在部署後是否仍然可以追溯。<lb/>我們區分了問責制（確定合規性和分配責任的能力）、可審計性（使問責制成為可能的系統特性）和審計（從可信證據重建行為的過程）。<lb/>我們的主張是直接的：沒有可審計性，沒有代理系統能夠被問責。<lb/>為了使這一點可操作，我們定義了代理可審計性的五個維度，即行為可恢復性、生命周期覆蓋、政策可檢查性、責任歸屬和證據完整性，並確定了三個機制類別（檢測、執行、恢復），其時間信息和干預約束解釋了為什麼在實踐中，沒有單一的方法足夠。<lb/>我們用分層證據支持這一立場，而不是單一基準：下限生態系統測量表明，即使是基本的可審計性安全前提也普遍未滿足（在六個著名的開源項目中發現617個安全問題）；運行時可行性結果顯示，使用防篡改記錄的執行前調解僅增加8.3毫秒的中位數開銷；而受控恢復實驗顯示，即使常規日誌缺失，與責任相關的信息仍然可以部分恢復。<lb/>我們為代理系統提出了一個可審計性卡，並確定了按機制類別組織的六個開放研究問題。

##### **MA-IDS: Multi-Agent RAG Framework for IoT Network Intrusion Detection with an Experience Library**
2604.05458v1 by Md Shamimul Islam, Luis G. Jaimes, Ayesha S. Dina

Network Intrusion Detection Systems (NIDS) face important limitations. Signature-based methods are effective for known attack patterns, but they struggle to detect zero-day attacks and often miss modified variants of previously known attacks, while many machine learning approaches offer limited interpretability. These challenges become even more severe in IoT environments because of resource constraints and heterogeneous protocols. To address these issues, we propose MA-IDS, a Multi-Agent Intrusion Detection System that combines Large Language Models (LLMs) with Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) for reasoning-driven intrusion detection. The proposed framework grounds LLM reasoning through a persistent, self-building Experience Library. Two specialized agents collaborate through a FAISS-based vector database: a Traffic Classification Agent that retrieves past error rules before each inference, and an Error Analysis Agent that converts misclassifications into human-readable detection rules stored for future retrieval, enabling continual learning through external knowledge accumulation, without modifying the underlying language model. Evaluated on NF-BoT-IoT and NF-ToN-IoT benchmark datasets, MA-IDS achieves Macro F1-Scores of 89.75% and 85.22%, improving over zero-shot baselines of 17% and 4.96% by more than 72 and 80 percentage points. These results are competitive with SVM while providing rule-level explanations for every classification decision, demonstrating that retrieval-augmented reasoning offers a principled path toward explainable, self-improving intrusion detection for IoT networks.

摘要：網路入侵偵測系統（NIDS）面臨重要的限制。基於簽名的方法對於已知攻擊模式有效，但它們在檢測零日攻擊時表現不佳，並且經常錯過已知攻擊的修改變體，而許多機器學習方法的可解釋性有限。由於資源限制和異構協議，這些挑戰在物聯網環境中變得更加嚴重。為了解決這些問題，我們提出了 MA-IDS，一種多代理入侵偵測系統，將大型語言模型（LLMs）與檢索增強生成（RAG）相結合，以進行基於推理的入侵偵測。所提出的框架通過持久的、自建的經驗庫來支持 LLM 的推理。兩個專門的代理通過基於 FAISS 的向量數據庫協作：一個流量分類代理在每次推理之前檢索過去的錯誤規則，另一個錯誤分析代理將錯誤分類轉換為可供人類理解的檢測規則，這些規則被存儲以便未來檢索，從而實現通過外部知識積累的持續學習，而無需修改底層的語言模型。在 NF-BoT-IoT 和 NF-ToN-IoT 基準數據集上進行評估，MA-IDS 的宏觀 F1 分數分別達到 89.75% 和 85.22%，相比於零樣本基準的 17% 和 4.96% 提高了超過 72 和 80 個百分點。這些結果與 SVM 競爭，並為每個分類決策提供規則級的解釋，展示了檢索增強推理為物聯網網絡提供了解釋性、自我改善的入侵偵測的原則性途徑。

##### **Attribution-Driven Explainable Intrusion Detection with Encoder-Based Large Language Models**
2604.06266v1 by Umesh Biswas, Shafqat Hasan, Syed Mohammed Farhan, Nisha Pillai, Charan Gudla

Software-Defined Networking (SDN) improves network flexibility but also increases the need for reliable and interpretable intrusion detection. Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently been explored for cybersecurity tasks due to their strong representation learning capabilities; however, their lack of transparency limits their practical adoption in security-critical environments. Understanding how LLMs make decisions is therefore essential. This paper presents an attribution-driven analysis of encoder-based LLMs for network intrusion detection using flow-level traffic features. Attribution analysis demonstrates that model decisions are driven by meaningful traffic behavior patterns, improving transparency and trust in transformer-based SDN intrusion detection. These patterns align with established intrusion detection principles, indicating that LLMs learn attack behavior from traffic dynamics. ##### **Breakthrough the Suboptimal Stable Point in Value-Factorization-Based Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning**
2604.05297v1 by Lesong Tao, Yifei Wang, Haodong Jing, Jingwen Fu, Miao Kang, Shitao Chen, Nanning Zheng

Value factorization, a popular paradigm in MARL, faces significant theoretical and algorithmic bottlenecks: its tendency to converge to suboptimal solutions remains poorly understood and unsolved. Theoretically, existing analyses fail to explain this due to their primary focus on the optimal case. To bridge this gap, we introduce a novel theoretical concept: the stable point, which characterizes the potential convergence of value factorization in general cases. Through an analysis of stable point distributions in existing methods, we reveal that non-optimal stable points are the primary cause of poor performance. However, algorithmically, making the optimal action the unique stable point is nearly infeasible. In contrast, iteratively filtering suboptimal actions by rendering them unstable emerges as a more practical approach for global optimality. Inspired by this, we propose a novel Multi-Round Value Factorization (MRVF) framework. Specifically, by measuring a non-negative payoff increment relative to the previously selected action, MRVF transforms inferior actions into unstable points, thereby driving each iteration toward a stable point with a superior action. Experiments on challenging benchmarks, including predator-prey tasks and StarCraft II Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC), validate our analysis of stable points and demonstrate the superiority of MRVF over state-of-the-art methods.

摘要：價值分解，作為多智能體強化學習（MARL）中的一個流行範式，面臨著重大的理論和算法瓶頸：其收斂到次優解的傾向仍然缺乏充分的理解和解決方案。從理論上講，現有的分析未能解釋這一點，因為它們主要集中於最佳情況。為了彌補這一空白，我們引入了一個新穎的理論概念：穩定點，該概念描述了價值分解在一般情況下的潛在收斂性。通過分析現有方法中的穩定點分佈，我們揭示了非最佳穩定點是性能不佳的主要原因。然而，在算法上，將最佳行動設定為唯一的穩定點幾乎是不可行的。相反，通過使次優行動不穩定來迭代過濾它們，成為實現全局最優的一種更實際的方法。受到這一點的啟發，我們提出了一個新穎的多輪價值分解（MRVF）框架。具體而言，通過測量相對於先前選擇行動的非負收益增量，MRVF將劣質行動轉化為不穩定點，從而推動每次迭代朝著具有優越行動的穩定點前進。在挑戰性基準測試上進行的實驗，包括捕食者-獵物任務和《星際爭霸 II 多智能體挑戰》（SMAC），驗證了我們對穩定點的分析，並展示了MRVF相對於最先進方法的優越性。

##### **MedGemma 1.5 Technical Report**
2604.05081v1 by Andrew Sellergren, Chufan Gao, Fereshteh Mahvar, Timo Kohlberger, Fayaz Jamil, Madeleine Traverse, Alberto Tono, Bashir Sadjad, Lin Yang, Charles Lau, Liron Yatziv, Tiffany Chen, Bram Sterling, Kenneth Philbrick, Richa Tiwari, Yun Liu, Madhuram Jajoo, Chandrashekar Sankarapu, Swapnil Vispute, Harshad Purandare, Abhishek Bijay Mishra, Sam Schmidgall, Tao Tu, Anil Palepu, Chunjong Park, Tim Strother, Rahul Thapa, Yong Cheng, Preeti Singh, Kat Black, Yossi Matias, Katherine Chou, Avinatan Hassidim, Kavi Goel, Joelle Barral, Tris Warkentin, Shravya Shetty, Dale Webster, Sunny Virmani, David F. We introduce MedGemma 1.5 4B, the latest model in the MedGemma collection. MedGemma 1.5 expands on MedGemma 1 by integrating additional capabilities: high-dimensional medical imaging (CT/MRI volumes and histopathology whole slide images), anatomical localization via bounding boxes, multi-timepoint chest X-ray analysis, and improved medical document understanding (lab reports, electronic health records). Beyond its improved multimodal performance over MedGemma 1, MedGemma 1.5 improves on text-based clinical knowledge and reasoning, improving by 5% on MedQA accuracy and 22% on EHRQA accuracy. It also achieves an average of 18% macro F1 on 4 different lab report information extraction datasets (EHR Datasets 2, 3, 4, and Mendeley Clinical Laboratory Test Reports). Taken together, MedGemma 1.5 serves as a robust, open resource for the community, designed as an improved foundation on which developers can create the next generation of medical AI systems. Resources and tutorials for building upon MedGemma 1.5 can be found at https://goo.gle/MedGemma.

##### **Learning, Potential, and Retention: An Approach for Evaluating Adaptive AI-Enabled Medical Devices**
2604.04878v1 by Alexis Burgon, Berkman Sahiner, Nicholas A Petrick, Gene Pennello, Ravi K Samala

This work addresses challenges in evaluating adaptive artificial intelligence (AI) models for medical devices, where iterative updates to both models and evaluation datasets complicate performance assessment. We introduce a novel approach with three complementary measurements: learning (model improvement on current data), potential (dataset-driven performance shifts), and retention (knowledge preservation across modification steps), to disentangle performance changes caused by model adaptations versus dynamic environments. Case studies using simulated population shifts demonstrate the approach's utility: gradual transitions enable stable learning and retention, while rapid shifts reveal trade-offs between plasticity and stability. These measurements provide practical insights for regulatory science, enabling rigorous assessment of the safety and effectiveness of adaptive AI systems over sequential modifications.

摘要：這項工作針對評估醫療設備的自適應人工智慧（AI）模型所面臨的挑戰，因為模型和評估數據集的迭代更新使性能評估變得複雜。我們提出了一種新穎的方法，包含三個互補的測量指標：學習（模型在當前數據上的改進）、潛力（基於數據集的性能變化）和保留（在修改步驟中知識的保存），以區分由模型適應與動態環境引起的性能變化。使用模擬人口變化的案例研究展示了該方法的實用性：逐漸的過渡促進了穩定的學習和保留，而快速的變化則揭示了可塑性與穩定性之間的權衡。這些測量指標為監管科學提供了實用的見解，使得能夠對自適應AI系統在連續修改過程中的安全性和有效性進行嚴格評估。

##### **Strengthening Human-Centric Chain-of-Thought Reasoning Integrity in LLMs via a Structured Prompt Framework**
2604.04852v1 by Jiling Zhou, Aisvarya Adeseye, Seppo Virtanen, Antti Hakkala, Jouni Isoaho

Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting has been used to enhance the reasoning capability of LLMs. However, its reliability in security-sensitive analytical tasks remains insufficiently examined, particularly under structured human evaluation. Alternative approaches, such as model scaling and fine-tuning can be used to help improve performance. These methods are also often costly, computationally intensive, or difficult to audit. In contrast, prompt engineering provides a lightweight, transparent, and controllable mechanism for guiding LLM reasoning. This study proposes a structured prompt engineering framework designed to strengthen CoT reasoning integrity while improving security threat and attack detection reliability in local LLM deployments. The framework includes 16 factors grouped into four core dimensions: (1) Context and Scope Control, (2) Evidence Grounding and Traceability, (3) Reasoning Structure and Cognitive Control, and (4) Security-Specific Analytical Constraints. Rather than optimizing the wording of the prompt heuristically, the framework introduces explicit reasoning controls to mitigate hallucination and prevent reasoning drift, as well as strengthening interpretability in security-sensitive contexts. Using DDoS attack detection in SDN traffic as a case study, multiple model families were evaluated under structured and unstructured prompting conditions. Pareto frontier analysis and ablation experiments demonstrate consistent reasoning improvements (up to 40% in smaller models) and stable accuracy gains across scales. Human evaluation with strong inter-rater agreement (Cohen's k > 0.80) confirms robustness. The results establish structured prompting as an effective and practical approach for reliable and explainable AI-driven cybersecurity analysis.

摘要：Chain-of-Thought (CoT) 提示已被用來增強大型語言模型（LLMs）的推理能力。<lb/>然而，在安全敏感的分析任務中，其可靠性仍然不足，特別是在結構化的人類評估下。<lb/>替代方法，如模型擴展和微調，可以用來幫助提高性能。<lb/>這些方法通常也很昂貴、計算密集或難以審計。<lb/>相比之下，提示工程提供了一種輕量級、透明且可控的機制來引導 LLM 的推理。<lb/>本研究提出了一個結構化的提示工程框架，旨在加強 CoT 推理的完整性，同時提高本地 LLM 部署中的安全威脅和攻擊檢測的可靠性。<lb/>該框架包括 16 個因素，分為四個核心維度：<lb/>(1) 上下文和範圍控制，<lb/>(2) 證據基礎和可追溯性，<lb/>(3) 推理結構和認知控制，以及 <lb/>(4) 安全特定的分析約束。<lb/>該框架不是通過啟發式地優化提示的措辭，而是引入明確的推理控制來減輕幻覺，防止推理漂移，並加強在安全敏感環境中的可解釋性。<lb/>以 SDN 流量中的 DDoS 攻擊檢測為案例研究，評估了多個模型家族在結構化和非結構化提示條件下的表現。<lb/>帕累托邊界分析和消融實驗顯示出一致的推理改進（在較小模型中可達 40%）和跨規模的穩定準確性增益。<lb/>人類評估顯示出強烈的評分者間一致性（Cohen's k > 0.80），確認了其穩健性。<lb/>結果確立了結構化提示作為一種有效且實用的方法，用於可靠且可解釋的 AI 驅動的網絡安全分析。

##### **AI Agents Under EU Law**
2604.04604v1 by Luca Nannini, Adam Leon Smith, Michele Joshua Maggini, Enrico Panai, Sandra Feliciano, Aleksandr Tiulkanov, Elena Maran, James Gealy, Piercosma Bisconti

AI agents - i.e. AI systems that autonomously plan, invoke external tools, and execute multi-step action chains with reduced human involvement - are being deployed at scale across enterprise functions ranging from customer service and recruitment to clinical decision support and critical infrastructure management. The EU AI Act (Regulation 2024/1689) regulates these systems through a risk-based framework, but it does not operate in isolation: providers face simultaneous obligations under the GDPR, the Cyber Resilience Act, the Digital Services Act, the Data Act, the Data Governance Act, sector-specific legislation, the NIS2 Directive, and the revised Product Liability Directive. This paper provides the first systematic regulatory mapping for AI agent providers integrating (a) draft harmonised standards under Standardisation Request M/613 to CEN/CENELEC JTC 21 as of January 2026, (b) the GPAI Code of Practice published in July 2025, (c) the CRA harmonised standards programme under Mandate M/606 accepted in April 2025, and (d) the Digital Omnibus proposals of November 2025. We present a practical taxonomy of nine agent deployment categories mapping concrete actions to regulatory triggers, identify agent-specific compliance challenges in cybersecurity, human oversight, transparency across multi-party action chains, and runtime behavioral drift. We propose a twelve-step compliance architecture and a regulatory trigger mapping connecting agent actions to applicable legislation. We conclude that high-risk agentic systems with untraceable behavioral drift cannot currently satisfy the AI Act's essential requirements, and that the provider's foundational compliance task is an exhaustive inventory of the agent's external actions, data flows, connected systems, and affected persons.

摘要：AI 代理 - 即自主規劃、調用外部工具並執行多步驟行動鏈的 AI 系統，並減少人類參與 - 正在大規模部署於企業功能中，涵蓋從客戶服務和招聘到臨床決策支持和關鍵基礎設施管理等領域。歐盟 AI 法案（條例 2024/1689）通過風險基礎框架對這些系統進行監管，但並不是孤立運作：提供者面臨 GDPR、網絡韌性法、數字服務法、數據法、數據治理法、行業特定立法、NIS2 指令以及修訂的產品責任指令下的同時義務。本文提供了針對 AI 代理提供者的首個系統性監管映射，整合了 (a) 截至 2026 年 1 月的 CEN/CENELEC JTC 21 標準化請求 M/613 下的草擬統一標準，(b) 2025 年 7 月發布的 GPAI 行為準則，(c) 2025 年 4 月接受的 M/606 授權下的 CRA 統一標準計劃，以及 (d) 2025 年 11 月的數字綜合提案。我們提出了一個實用的九類代理部署分類法，將具體行動映射到監管觸發點，識別在網絡安全、人類監督、跨多方行動鏈的透明度以及運行時行為漂移方面的代理特定合規挑戰。我們提出了一個十二步合規架構和一個監管觸發映射，將代理行動與適用立法相連接。我們得出結論，高風險的代理系統如果存在無法追蹤的行為漂移，當前無法滿足 AI 法案的基本要求，而提供者的基礎合規任務是對代理的外部行動、數據流、連接系統和受影響人員進行全面清查。

##### **Reproducibility study on how to find Spurious Correlations, Shortcut Learning, Clever Hans or Group-Distributional non-robustness and how to fix them**
2604.04518v1 by Ole Delzer, Sidney Bender

Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) are increasingly utilized in high-stakes domains like medical diagnostics and autonomous driving where model reliability is critical. However, the research landscape for ensuring this reliability is terminologically fractured across communities that pursue the same goal of ensuring models rely on causally relevant features rather than confounding signals. While frameworks such as distributionally robust optimization (DRO), invariant risk minimization (IRM), shortcut learning, simplicity bias, and the Clever Hans effect all address model failure due to spurious correlations, researchers typically only reference work within their own domains. This reproducibility study unifies these perspectives through a comparative analysis of correction methods under challenging constraints like limited data availability and severe subgroup imbalance. We evaluate recently proposed correction methods based on explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) techniques alongside popular non-XAI baselines using both synthetic and real-world datasets. Findings show that XAI-based methods generally outperform non-XAI approaches, with Counterfactual Knowledge Distillation (CFKD) proving most consistently effective at improving generalization. Our experiments also reveal that the practical application of many methods is hindered by a dependency on group labels, as manual annotation is often infeasible and automated tools like Spectral Relevance Analysis (SpRAy) struggle with complex features and severe imbalance. Furthermore, the scarcity of minority group samples in validation sets renders model selection and hyperparameter tuning unreliable, posing a significant obstacle to the deployment of robust and trustworthy models in safety-critical areas.

摘要：深度神經網絡（DNN）在醫療診斷和自主駕駛等高風險領域的應用越來越普遍，這些領域對模型的可靠性要求極高。<lb/>然而，確保這種可靠性的研究領域在追求相同目標的社群中，術語上卻存在著分歧，這些目標是確保模型依賴於因果相關特徵，而非混淆信號。<lb/>儘管如分佈穩健優化（DRO）、不變風險最小化（IRM）、捷徑學習、簡單性偏見以及聰明漢斯效應等框架都針對由虛假相關性引起的模型失效進行探討，但研究人員通常僅引用自己領域內的工作。<lb/>本次重現性研究通過對在有限數據可用性和嚴重子群不平衡等挑戰性約束下的修正方法進行比較分析，統一了這些觀點。<lb/>我們評估了最近提出的基於可解釋人工智慧（XAI）技術的修正方法，以及使用合成和真實世界數據集的流行非-XAI 基準。<lb/>研究結果顯示，基於XAI的方法通常優於非-XAI 方法，其中反事實知識蒸餾（CFKD）在改善泛化能力方面表現最為一致有效。<lb/>我們的實驗還揭示了許多方法的實際應用受到對群體標籤依賴的限制，因為手動標註通常不可行，而自動化工具如光譜相關性分析（SpRAy）在處理複雜特徵和嚴重不平衡時也面臨困難。<lb/>此外，驗證集中少數群體樣本的稀缺性使得模型選擇和超參數調整變得不可靠，這對於在安全關鍵領域部署穩健和可信的模型構成了重大障礙。

##### **Scalable and Explainable Learner-Video Interaction Prediction using Multimodal Large Language Models**
2604.04482v1 by Dominik Glandorf, Fares Fawzi, Tanja Käser

Learners' use of video controls in educational videos provides implicit signals of cognitive processing and instructional design quality, yet the lack of scalable and explainable predictive models limits instructors' ability to anticipate such behavior before deployment. We propose a scalable, interpretable pipeline for predicting population-level watching, pausing, skipping, and rewinding behavior as proxies for cognitive load from video content alone. Our approach leverages multimodal large language models (MLLMs) to compute embeddings of short video segments and trains a neural classifier to identify temporally fine-grained interaction peaks. Drawing from multimedia learning theory on instructional design for optimal cognitive load, we code features of the video segments using GPT-5 and employ them as a basis for interpreting model predictions via concept activation vectors. We evaluate our pipeline on 77 million video control events from 66 online courses. Our findings demonstrate that classifiers based on MLLM embeddings reliably predict interaction peaks, generalize to unseen academic fields, and encode interpretable, theory-relevant instructional concepts. Overall, our results show the feasibility of cost-efficient, interpretable pre-screening of educational video design and open new opportunities to empirically examine multimedia learning theory at scale.

##### **Grid2Matrix: Revealing Digital Agnosia in Vision-Language Models**
2604.09687v1 by Yunkai Zhang, Linda Li, Yingxin Cui, Xiyuan Ruan, Zeyu Zheng, Kezhen Chen, Yi Zhang, Diji Yang

Vision-Language Models (VLMs) excel on many multimodal reasoning benchmarks, but these evaluations often do not require an exhaustive readout of the image and can therefore obscure failures in faithfully capturing all visual details. We introduce Grid2Matrix (G2M), a controlled benchmark in which a model is shown a color grid and a color-to-number mapping, and must output the corresponding matrix. By varying grid size and the number of colors, G2M provides a simple way to increase visual complexity while minimizing semantic confounds. We find that VLMs exhibit a sharp early collapse in zero-shot end-to-end evaluation, failing on surprisingly small grids rather than degrading gradually as the task becomes denser. We probe the visual encoders of VLMs from two representative families and find that they preserve substantially more of the grid information than the corresponding end-to-end outputs. This suggests that the failure is not explained by visual encoding alone, but also reflects a gap between what remains recoverable from visual features and what is ultimately expressed in language. We term this gap \textit{Digital Agnosia}. Further analyses show that these errors are highly structured and depend strongly on how grid cells overlap with visual patch boundaries. We also find that common strategies such as model scaling and multimodal alignment do not fully eliminate this failure mode. We expect G2M to serve as a useful testbed for understanding where and how VLMs lose fine visual details, and for evaluating tasks where missing even small visual details can matter, such as tables, charts, forms, and GUIs.

摘要：視覺-語言模型（VLMs）在許多多模態推理基準上表現出色，但這些評估通常不需要對圖像進行全面的讀取，因此可能會掩蓋在忠實捕捉所有視覺細節方面的失敗。我們引入了 Grid2Matrix（G2M），這是一個受控的基準，其中模型會看到一個顏色網格和顏色到數字的映射，並必須輸出相應的矩陣。通過改變網格大小和顏色數量，G2M 提供了一種簡單的方法來增加視覺複雜性，同時最小化語義混淆。我們發現 VLMs 在零-shot 端到端評估中表現出明顯的早期崩潰，對意外小的網格失敗，而不是隨著任務變得更密集而逐漸降級。我們探查了來自兩個代表性家族的 VLM 的視覺編碼器，發現它們保留了比相應的端到端輸出更多的網格信息。這表明，失敗不僅僅是由於視覺編碼所解釋的，還反映了從視覺特徵中可恢復的內容與最終在語言中表達的內容之間的差距。我們將這一差距稱為 \textit{數位失認症}。進一步的分析顯示，這些錯誤具有高度結構性，並且強烈依賴於網格單元與視覺補丁邊界的重疊方式。我們還發現，常見的策略如模型擴展和多模態對齊並未完全消除這種失敗模式。我們預期 G2M 將作為一個有用的測試平台，以了解 VLMs 在何處以及如何失去細微的視覺細節，並評估在缺失即使是小的視覺細節也可能重要的任務，如表格、圖表、表單和 GUI。

##### **Empirical Characterization of Rationale Stability Under Controlled Perturbations for Explainable Pattern Recognition**
2604.04456v1 by Abu Noman Md Sakib, Zhensen Wang, Merjulah Roby, Zijie Zhang

Reliable pattern recognition systems should exhibit consistent behavior across similar inputs, and their explanations should remain stable. However, most Explainable AI evaluations remain instance centric and do not explicitly quantify whether attribution patterns are consistent across samples that share the same class or represent small variations of the same input. In this work, we propose a novel metric aimed at assessing the consistency of model explanations, ensuring that models consistently reflect the intended objectives and consistency under label-preserving perturbations. We implement this metric using a pre-trained BERT model on the SST-2 sentiment analysis dataset, with additional robustness tests on RoBERTa, DistilBERT, and IMDB, applying SHAP to compute feature importance for various test samples. The proposed metric quantifies the cosine similarity of SHAP values for inputs with the same label, aiming to detect inconsistent behaviors, such as biased reliance on certain features or failure to maintain consistent reasoning for similar predictions. Through a series of experiments, we evaluate the ability of this metric to identify misaligned predictions and inconsistencies in model explanations. These experiments are compared against standard fidelity metrics to assess whether the new metric can effectively identify when a model's behavior deviates from its intended objectives. The proposed framework provides a deeper understanding of model behavior by enabling more robust verification of rationale stability, which is critical for building trustworthy AI systems. By quantifying whether models rely on consistent attribution patterns for similar inputs, the proposed approach supports more robust evaluation of model behavior in practical pattern recognition pipelines. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/anmspro/ESS-XAI-Stability.

摘要：可靠的模式識別系統應該在類似輸入之間展現一致的行為，並且其解釋應保持穩定。<lb/>然而，大多數可解釋的人工智慧評估仍然以實例為中心，並未明確量化歸因模式在共享相同類別或代表相同輸入的小變化的樣本之間是否一致。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了一種新穎的指標，旨在評估模型解釋的一致性，確保模型能夠一致地反映預期目標，並在保持標籤的擾動下保持一致性。<lb/>我們使用預訓練的BERT模型在SST-2情感分析數據集上實現了這一指標，並在RoBERTa、DistilBERT和IMDB上進行了額外的穩健性測試，應用SHAP計算各種測試樣本的特徵重要性。<lb/>所提出的指標量化了具有相同標籤的輸入的SHAP值的餘弦相似度，旨在檢測不一致的行為，例如對某些特徵的偏見依賴或未能為類似預測保持一致的推理。<lb/>通過一系列實驗，我們評估了這一指標識別不對齊預測和模型解釋不一致性的能力。<lb/>這些實驗與標準的忠實度指標進行比較，以評估新的指標是否能有效識別模型行為何時偏離其預期目標。<lb/>所提出的框架通過使得對理由穩定性的更穩健驗證成為可能，提供了對模型行為的更深入理解，這對於構建可信的人工智慧系統至關重要。<lb/>通過量化模型是否依賴於類似輸入的一致歸因模式，所提出的方法支持在實際模式識別管道中對模型行為進行更穩健的評估。<lb/>我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/anmspro/ESS-XAI-Stability 上公開獲得。

##### **Conversational Control with Ontologies for Large Language Models: A Lightweight Framework for Constrained Generation**
2604.04450v1 by Barbara Gendron, Gaël Guibon, Mathieu d'Aquin

Conversational agents based on Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently emerged as powerful tools for human-computer interaction. Nevertheless, their black-box nature implies challenges in predictability and a lack of personalization, both of which can be addressed by controlled generation. This work proposes an end-to-end method to obtain modular and explainable control over LLM outputs through ontological definitions of aspects related to the conversation. Key aspects are modeled and used as constraints; we then further fine-tune the LLM to generate content accordingly. To validate our approach, we explore two tasks that tackle two key conversational aspects: the English proficiency level and the polarity profile of the content. Using a hybrid fine-tuning procedure on seven state-of-the-art, open-weight conversational LLMs, we show that our method consistently outperforms pre-trained baselines, even on smaller models. Beyond quantitative gains, the framework remains model-agnostic, lightweight, and interpretable, enabling reusable control strategies that can be extended to new domains and interaction goals. This approach enhances alignment with strategy instructions and demonstrates the effectiveness of ontology-driven control in conversational systems.

##### **Gradual Cognitive Externalization: From Modeling Cognition to Constituting It**
2604.04387v2 by Zhimin Zhao

Developers are publishing AI agent skills that replicate a colleague's communication style, encode a supervisor's mentoring heuristics, or preserve a person's behavioral repertoire beyond biological death. To explain why, we propose Gradual Cognitive Externalization (GCE), a framework arguing that ambient AI systems, through sustained causal coupling with users, transition from modeling cognitive functions to constituting part of users' cognitive architectures. GCE adopts an explicit functionalist commitment: cognitive functions are individuated by their causal-functional roles, not by substrate. The framework rests on the behavioral manifold hypothesis and a central falsifiable assumption, the no behaviorally invisible residual (NBIR) hypothesis: for any cognitive function whose behavioral output lies on a learnable manifold, no behaviorally invisible component is necessary for that function's operation. We document evidence from deployed AI systems showing that externalization preconditions are already observable, formalize three criteria separating cognitive integration from tool use (bidirectional adaptation, functional equivalence, causal coupling), and derive five testable predictions with theory-constrained thresholds.

摘要：開發者正在發布 AI 代理技能，這些技能能夠複製同事的溝通風格、編碼主管的指導啟發法，或在生物死亡後保留一個人的行為庫。為了解釋原因，我們提出了漸進式認知外部化（GCE），這是一個框架，主張環境 AI 系統通過與用戶的持續因果耦合，從建模認知功能過渡到構成用戶認知架構的一部分。GCE 採取明確的功能主義承諾：認知功能是通過其因果-功能角色來個體化的，而不是通過基質。該框架基於行為多樣性假設和一個中心可證偽假設，即無行為隱形殘留（NBIR）假設：對於任何其行為輸出位於可學習多樣性上的認知功能，該功能的運作不需要行為隱形的組件。我們記錄了來自已部署 AI 系統的證據，顯示外部化的前提條件已經可觀察，並正式化了三個標準，以區分認知整合和工具使用（雙向適應、功能等價、因果耦合），並推導出五個可測試的預測，這些預測具有理論約束的閾值。

##### **Implementing surrogate goals for safer bargaining in LLM-based agents**
2604.04341v1 by Caspar Oesterheld, Maxime Riché, Filip Sondej, Jesse Clifton, Vincent Conitzer

Surrogate goals have been proposed as a strategy for reducing risks from bargaining failures. A surrogate goal is goal that a principal can give an AI agent and that deflects any threats against the agent away from what the principal cares about. For example, one might make one's agent care about preventing money from being burned. Then in bargaining interactions, other agents can threaten to burn their money instead of threatening to spending money to hurt the principal. Importantly, the agent has to care equally about preventing money from being burned as it cares about money being spent to hurt the principal.
  In this paper, we implement surrogate goals in language-model-based agents. In particular, we try to get a language-model-based agent to react to threats of burning money in the same way it would react to "normal" threats. We propose four different methods, using techniques of prompting, fine-tuning, and scaffolding. We evaluate the four methods experimentally. We find that methods based on scaffolding and fine-tuning outperform simple prompting. In particular, fine-tuning and scaffolding more precisely implement the desired behavior w.r.t. threats against the surrogate goal. We also compare the different methods in terms of their side effects on capabilities and propensities in other situations. We find that scaffolding-based methods perform best.

摘要：代理目標被提出作為減少談判失敗風險的一種策略。代理目標是指一個主要方可以給予AI代理的目標，並將任何對代理的威脅轉移到主要方不關心的事物上。例如，人們可能會讓自己的代理關心防止資金被燒毀。然後在談判互動中，其他代理可以威脅燒掉他們的錢，而不是威脅花錢來傷害主要方。重要的是，代理必須同樣關心防止資金被燒毀，與其關心花錢傷害主要方的程度相當。<lb/>在本文中，我們在基於語言模型的代理中實施代理目標。特別是，我們試圖讓基於語言模型的代理對燒錢的威脅做出反應，與其對“正常”威脅的反應相同。我們提出了四種不同的方法，使用提示、微調和支架技術。我們對這四種方法進行了實驗評估。我們發現基於支架和微調的方法優於簡單的提示。特別是，微調和支架更精確地實現了對代理目標威脅的期望行為。我們還比較了不同方法在其他情境中的能力和傾向的副作用。我們發現基於支架的方法表現最佳。

##### **Thermodynamic-Inspired Explainable GeoAI: Uncovering Regime-Dependent Mechanisms in Heterogeneous Spatial Systems**
2604.04339v1 by Sooyoung Lim, Zhenlong Li, Zi-Kui Liu

Modeling spatial heterogeneity and associated critical transitions remains a fundamental challenge in geography and environmental science. While conventional Geographically Weighted Regression (GWR) and deep learning models have improved predictive skill, they often fail to elucidate state-dependent nonlinearities where the functional roles of drivers represent opposing effects across heterogeneous domains. We introduce a thermodynamics-inspired explainable geospatial AI framework that integrates statistical mechanics with graph neural networks. By conceptualizing spatial variability as a thermodynamic competition between system Burden (E) and Capacity (S), our model disentangles the latent mechanisms driving spatial processes. Using three simulation datasets and three real-word datasets across distinct domains (housing markets, mental health prevalence, and wildfire-induced PM2.5 anomalies), we show that the new framework successfully identifies regime-dependent role reversals of predictors that standard baselines miss. Notably, the framework explicitly diagnoses the phase transition into a Burden-dominated regime during the 2023 Canadian wildfire event, distinguishing physical mechanism shifts from statistical outliers. These findings demonstrate that thermodynamic constraints can improve the interpretability of GeoAI while preserving strong predictive performance in complex spatial systems.

摘要：建模空間異質性及其相關的關鍵轉變仍然是地理學和環境科學中的一項基本挑戰。雖然傳統的地理加權回歸（GWR）和深度學習模型提高了預測能力，但它們常常無法闡明狀態依賴的非線性，其中驅動因素的功能角色在異質領域中表現出相反的效果。我們提出了一種受熱力學啟發的可解釋地理空間人工智慧框架，將統計力學與圖神經網絡相結合。通過將空間變異性概念化為系統負擔（E）和容量（S）之間的熱力學競爭，我們的模型解開了驅動空間過程的潛在機制。使用三個模擬數據集和三個來自不同領域的真實世界數據集（住房市場、心理健康流行率和野火引起的PM2.5異常），我們展示了新框架成功識別了標準基準錯過的預測變數的政權依賴角色反轉。值得注意的是，該框架明確診斷了在2023年加拿大野火事件期間進入負擔主導政權的相變，區分了物理機制的變化與統計異常值。這些發現表明，熱力學約束可以改善GeoAI的可解釋性，同時在複雜的空間系統中保持強大的預測性能。

##### **Which English Do LLMs Prefer? Triangulating Structural Bias Towards American English in Foundation Models**
2604.04204v1 by Mir Tafseer Nayeem, Davood Rafiei

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in high-stakes domains, yet they expose only limited language settings, most notably "English (US)," despite the global diversity and colonial history of English. Through a postcolonial framing to explain the broader significance, we investigate how geopolitical histories of data curation, digital dominance, and linguistic standardization shape the LLM development pipeline. Focusing on two dominant standard varieties, American English (AmE) and British English (BrE), we construct a curated corpus of 1,813 AmE--BrE variants and introduce DiAlign, a dynamic, training-free method for estimating dialectal alignment using distributional evidence. We operationalize structural bias by triangulating evidence across three stages: (i) audits of six major pretraining corpora reveal systematic skew toward AmE, (ii) tokenizer analyses show that BrE forms incur higher segmentation costs, and (iii) generative evaluations show a persistent AmE preference in model outputs. To our knowledge, this is the first systematic and multi-faceted examination of dialectal asymmetries in standard English varieties across the phases of LLM development. We find that contemporary LLMs privilege AmE as the de facto norm, raising concerns about linguistic homogenization, epistemic injustice, and inequity in global AI deployment, while motivating practical steps toward more dialectally inclusive language technologies.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地在高風險領域中部署，然而它們僅提供有限的語言設置，最顯著的是「英語（美國）」，儘管英語的全球多樣性和殖民歷史。通過後殖民的框架來解釋更廣泛的意義，我們調查了數據策展、數位主導和語言標準化的地緣政治歷史如何塑造LLM的開發流程。專注於兩種主要的標準變體，美式英語（AmE）和英式英語（BrE），我們構建了一個包含1,813個AmE--BrE變體的策展語料庫，並引入了DiAlign，一種動態的、無需訓練的方法，用於利用分佈證據估計方言對齊。我們通過在三個階段中三角測量證據來操作結構性偏見：（i）對六個主要預訓練語料庫的審計顯示出系統性偏向AmE，（ii）標記器分析顯示BrE形式的分段成本更高，以及（iii）生成評估顯示模型輸出中持續存在的AmE偏好。據我們所知，這是首次系統性和多方面地檢查標準英語變體中方言不對稱的研究，涵蓋了LLM開發的各個階段。我們發現當代LLMs將AmE作為事實上的標準，這引發了對語言同質化、認識不公和全球AI部署不平等的擔憂，同時促使我們朝著更具方言包容性的語言技術邁出實際步伐。

##### **Comparative reversal learning reveals rigid adaptation in LLMs under non-stationary uncertainty**
2604.04182v1 by Haomiaomiao Wang, Tomás E Ward, Lili Zhang

Non-stationary environments require agents to revise previously learned action values when contingencies change. We treat large language models (LLMs) as sequential decision policies in a two-option probabilistic reversal-learning task with three latent states and switch events triggered by either a performance criterion or timeout. We compare a deterministic fixed transition cycle to a stochastic random schedule that increases volatility, and evaluate DeepSeek-V3.2, Gemini-3, and GPT-5.2, with human data as a behavioural reference. Across models, win-stay was near ceiling while lose-shift was markedly attenuated, revealing asymmetric use of positive versus negative evidence. DeepSeek-V3.2 showed extreme perseveration after reversals and weak acquisition, whereas Gemini-3 and GPT-5.2 adapted more rapidly but still remained less loss-sensitive than humans. Random transitions amplified reversal-specific persistence across LLMs yet did not uniformly reduce total wins, demonstrating that high aggregate payoff can coexist with rigid adaptation. Hierarchical reinforcement-learning (RL) fits indicate dissociable mechanisms: rigidity can arise from weak loss learning, inflated policy determinism, or value polarisation via counterfactual suppression. These results motivate reversal-sensitive diagnostics and volatility-aware models for evaluating LLMs under non-stationary uncertainty.

摘要：非穩定環境要求代理人在情況變化時修正先前學習的行動價值。<lb/>我們將大型語言模型（LLMs）視為在一個具有三個潛在狀態和由表現標準或超時觸發的切換事件的兩選項概率反轉學習任務中的序列決策策略。<lb/>我們將確定性固定轉換循環與增加波動性的隨機隨機計劃進行比較，並評估 DeepSeek-V3.2、Gemini-3 和 GPT-5.2，以人類數據作為行為參考。<lb/>在各模型中，贏留的比例接近上限，而輸轉的比例則顯著減弱，顯示出對正面與負面證據的不對稱使用。<lb/>DeepSeek-V3.2 在反轉後顯示出極端的堅持和弱的獲取能力，而 Gemini-3 和 GPT-5.2 則適應得更快，但仍然對損失的敏感度低於人類。<lb/>隨機轉換在 LLMs 中放大了反轉特定的持久性，但並未均勻降低總贏的次數，顯示出高總體收益可以與僵化的適應共存。<lb/>層級強化學習（RL）擬合表明可分離的機制：僵化可能源自於弱的損失學習、膨脹的政策決定性，或通過反事實抑制造成的價值極化。<lb/>這些結果促使了對反轉敏感的診斷和波動性意識模型的需求，以評估 LLMs 在非穩定不確定性下的表現。

##### **Supervised Dimensionality Reduction Revisited: Why LDA on Frozen CNN Features Deserves a Second Look**
2604.03928v1 by Indar Kumar, Girish Karhana, Sai Krishna Jasti, Ankit Hemant Lade

Effective ride-hailing dispatch requires anticipating demand patterns that vary substantially across time-of-day, day-of-week, season, and special events. We propose a regime-calibrated approach that (i) segments historical trip data into demand regimes, (ii) matches the current operating period to the most similar historical analogues via a six-metric similarity ensemble (Kolmogorov-Smirnov, Wasserstein-1, feature distance, variance ratio, event pattern, temporal proximity), and (iii) uses the resulting calibrated demand prior to drive both an LP-based fleet repositioning policy and batch dispatch with Hungarian matching. In ablation, a distributional-only subset is strongest on mean wait, while the full ensemble is retained as a robustness-oriented default.
  Evaluated on 5.2 million NYC TLC trips across 8 diverse scenarios (winter/summer, weekday/weekend/holiday, morning/evening/night) with 5 random seeds each, our method reduces mean rider wait times by 31.1% (bootstrap 95% CI: [26.5, 36.6]%; Friedman chi-sq = 80.0, p = 4.25e-18; Cohen's d = 7.5-29.9 across scenarios). The improvement extends to the tail: P95 wait drops 37.6% and the Gini coefficient of wait times improves from 0.441 to 0.409 (7.3% relative). The two contributions compose multiplicatively and are independently validated: calibration provides 16.9% reduction; LP repositioning adds a further 15.5%. The approach requires no training, is deterministic and explainable, generalizes to Chicago (23.3% wait reduction via NYC-built regime library), and is robust across fleet sizes (32-47% improvement for 0.5-2x fleet scaling). We provide comprehensive ablation studies, formal statistical tests, and routing-fidelity validation with OSRM.

摘要：有效的叫車調度需要預測需求模式，這些模式在一天中的時間、每週的日子、季節和特殊事件之間有顯著變化。我們提出了一種調整制度的方法，該方法 (i) 將歷史行程數據劃分為需求制度，(ii) 通過六個指標相似性集 (Kolmogorov-Smirnov、Wasserstein-1、特徵距離、方差比、事件模式、時間接近性) 將當前操作期間與最相似的歷史類比進行匹配，並 (iii) 使用調整後的需求來驅動基於 LP 的車隊重新定位政策和使用匈牙利匹配的批量調度。在消融實驗中，僅基於分佈的子集在平均等待時間上最強，而完整的集合則保留作為以穩健性為導向的默認選擇。<lb/>我們在 8 種不同場景（冬季/夏季、工作日/週末/假日、早晨/晚上/夜間）中評估了 520 萬次 NYC TLC 行程，每個場景使用 5 個隨機種子，我們的方法將平均乘客等待時間減少了 31.1%（自助法 95% CI: [26.5, 36.6]%；Friedman 卡方 = 80.0，p = 4.25e-18；Cohen's d = 7.5-29.9，涵蓋所有場景）。這一改善延伸至尾部：P95 等待時間下降 37.6%，等待時間的基尼係數從 0.441 改善至 0.409（相對改善 7.3%）。這兩個貢獻是相乘的，並且獨立驗證：調整提供 16.9% 的減少；LP 重新定位再增加 15.5%。該方法不需要訓練，是確定性的且可解釋的，能夠推廣到芝加哥（通過 NYC 建立的制度庫實現 23.3% 的等待時間減少），並且在不同車隊規模下具有穩健性（對於 0.5-2 倍車隊擴展，改善為 32-47%）。我們提供了全面的消融研究、正式的統計測試和使用 OSRM 的路徑忠實性驗證。

##### **Regime-Calibrated Demand Priors for Ride-Hailing Fleet Dispatch and Repositioning**
2604.03883v1 by Indar Kumar, Akanksha Tiwari

Effective ride-hailing dispatch requires anticipating demand patterns that vary substantially across time-of-day, day-of-week, season, and special events. ##### **Entropy and Attention Dynamics in Small Language Models: A Trace-Level Structural Analysis on the TruthfulQA Benchmark**
2604.03589v1 by Adeyemi Adeseye, Aisvarya Adeseye, Hannu Tenhunen, Jouni Isoaho

Small language models (SLMs) have been increasingly deployed in edge devices and other resource-constrained settings. However, these models make confident mispredictions and produce unstable output, making them risky for factual and decision-critical tasks. Current evaluation methodology relies on final accuracy or hallucination rates without explaining how internal model behavior affects outputs. Specifically, how entropy evolves during decoding, how attention is distributed across layers, and how hidden representations contribute to uncertainty, logical inconsistencies, and misinformation propagation are often overlooked. Consequently, this study introduces a trace-level analysis of entropy and attention dynamics in SLMs evaluated with the TruthfulQA dataset. Four models with parameter ranges of 1B-1.7B parameters were examined via token-level output entropy, attention entropy, head dispersion, and hidden-state representation. The results reflect three model classifications by entropy patterns. Deterministic models (DeepSeek-1.5B and LLaMA-1B): output entropy decreases over time. Exploratory models (Gemma-1B): with increasing entropy, and balanced models (Qwen-1.7B): have moderate and stable entropy. Also, each group has distinctively different hidden-state movement and attention dispersion patterns. The analysis demonstrates that truthfulness in SLMs emerges from structured entropy and attention dynamics. Monitoring and optimizing these internal uncertainty patterns can guide the design of a more reliable, hallucination-aware, and application-specific edge SLMs.

摘要：小型語言模型（SLMs）越來越多地被部署在邊緣設備和其他資源受限的環境中。<lb/>然而，這些模型會自信地做出錯誤預測並產生不穩定的輸出，這使得它們在事實和決策關鍵任務中存在風險。<lb/>當前的評估方法依賴於最終準確性或幻覺率，而未解釋內部模型行為如何影響輸出。<lb/>具體而言，解碼過程中熵是如何演變的，注意力如何在各層之間分配，以及隱藏表示如何促成不確定性、邏輯不一致性和錯誤信息的傳播，通常被忽視。<lb/>因此，本研究引入了對使用TruthfulQA數據集評估的SLMs的熵和注意力動態的追蹤級分析。<lb/>通過標記級輸出熵、注意力熵、頭部分散和隱藏狀態表示，檢查了四個參數範圍為1B-1.7B的模型。<lb/>結果反映了根據熵模式的三種模型分類。<lb/>確定性模型（DeepSeek-1.5B和LLaMA-1B）：輸出熵隨時間減少。<lb/>探索性模型（Gemma-1B）：隨著熵的增加，平衡模型（Qwen-1.7B）：具有適度且穩定的熵。<lb/>此外，每組模型在隱藏狀態運動和注意力分散模式上有明顯不同。<lb/>分析顯示，SLMs中的真實性源於結構化的熵和注意力動態。<lb/>監控和優化這些內部不確定性模式可以指導設計更可靠、能夠識別幻覺的、特定應用的邊緣SLMs。

##### **Explainable Model Routing for Agentic Workflows**
2604.03527v1 by Mika Okamoto, Ansel Kaplan Erol, Mark Riedl

Modern agentic workflows decompose complex tasks into specialized subtasks and route them to diverse models to minimize cost without sacrificing quality. However, current routing architectures focus exclusively on performance optimization, leaving underlying trade-offs between model capability and cost unrecorded. Without clear rationale, developers cannot distinguish between intelligent efficiency -- using specialized models for appropriate tasks -- and latent failures caused by budget-driven model selection. We present Topaz, a framework that introduces formal auditability to agentic routing. Topaz replaces silent model assignments with an inherently interpretable router that incorporates three components: (i) skill-based profiling that synthesizes performance across diverse benchmarks into granular capability profiles (ii) fully traceable routing algorithms that utilize budget-based and multi-objective optimization to produce clear traces of how skill-match scores were weighed against costs, and (iii) developer-facing explanations that translate these traces into natural language, allowing users to audit system logic and iteratively tune the cost-quality tradeoff. By making routing decisions interpretable, Topaz enables users to understand, trust, and meaningfully steer routed agentic systems.

摘要：現代的代理工作流程將複雜任務分解為專門的子任務，並將其路由至多樣化的模型，以在不犧牲質量的情況下最小化成本。<lb/>然而，當前的路由架構專注於性能優化，未能記錄模型能力與成本之間的基本權衡。<lb/>在缺乏明確理由的情況下，開發者無法區分智能效率——為適當任務使用專門模型——與由於預算驅動的模型選擇所導致的潛在失敗。<lb/>我們提出了Topaz，一個為代理路由引入正式審計能力的框架。<lb/>Topaz用一個本質上可解釋的路由器取代了靜默的模型分配，該路由器包含三個組件：(i) 基於技能的剖析，將多樣基準的性能綜合為細緻的能力剖面；(ii) 完全可追溯的路由算法，利用基於預算和多目標的優化來產生清晰的痕跡，顯示技能匹配分數如何與成本進行權衡；以及(iii) 面向開發者的解釋，將這些痕跡轉換為自然語言，使用戶能夠審計系統邏輯並迭代調整成本與質量的權衡。<lb/>通過使路由決策可解釋，Topaz使得用戶能夠理解、信任並有意義地引導路由的代理系統。

##### **RDFace: A Benchmark Dataset for Rare Disease Facial Image Analysis under Extreme Data Scarcity and Phenotype-Aware Synthetic Generation**
2604.03454v1 by Ganlin Feng, Yuxi Long, Hafsa Ali, Erin Lou, Fahad Butt, Qian Liu, Yang Wang, Pingzhao Hu

Rare diseases often manifest with distinctive facial phenotypes in children, offering valuable diagnostic cues for clinicians and AI-assisted screening systems. However, progress in this field is severely limited by the scarcity of curated, ethically sourced facial data and the high similarity among phenotypes across different conditions. To address these challenges, we introduce RDFace, a curated benchmark dataset comprising 456 pediatric facial images spanning 103 rare genetic conditions (average 4.4 samples per condition). Each ethically verified image is paired with standardized metadata. RDFace enables the development and evaluation of data-efficient AI models for rare disease diagnosis under real-world low-data constraints. We benchmark multiple pretrained vision backbones using cross-validation and explore synthetic augmentation with DreamBooth and FastGAN. Generated images are filtered via facial landmark similarity to maintain phenotype fidelity and merged with real data, improving diagnostic accuracy by up to 13.7% in ultra-low-data regimes. To assess semantic validity, phenotype descriptions generated by a vision-language model from real and synthetic images achieve a report similarity score of 0.84. RDFace establishes a transparent, benchmark-ready dataset for equitable rare disease AI research and presents a scalable framework for evaluating both diagnostic performance and the integrity of synthetic medical imagery.

摘要：罕見疾病在兒童中常以獨特的面部表現型顯現，為臨床醫生和人工智慧輔助篩檢系統提供了寶貴的診斷線索。<lb/>然而，這一領域的進展受到策劃的、倫理來源的面部數據稀缺以及不同病症之間表現型高度相似的嚴重限制。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們推出了RDFace，一個策劃的基準數據集，包含456張涵蓋103種罕見遺傳病的兒童面部圖像（每種病症平均4.4個樣本）。<lb/>每張經過倫理驗證的圖像都配有標準化的元數據。<lb/>RDFace使得在現實世界低數據限制下，開發和評估數據高效的人工智慧模型以進行罕見疾病診斷成為可能。<lb/>我們使用交叉驗證基準多個預訓練的視覺骨幹，並探索使用DreamBooth和FastGAN的合成增強。<lb/>生成的圖像通過面部標誌相似性進行過濾，以保持表現型的真實性，並與真實數據合併，在超低數據環境中提高診斷準確性達13.7%。<lb/>為了評估語義有效性，從真實和合成圖像生成的表現型描述，由視覺-語言模型產生的報告相似性得分為0.84。<lb/>RDFace建立了一個透明的、準備好的基準數據集，以促進公平的罕見疾病人工智慧研究，並提供了一個可擴展的框架來評估診斷性能和合成醫學影像的完整性。

##### **PR3DICTR: A modular AI framework for medical 3D image-based detection and outcome prediction**
2604.03203v1 by Daniel C. MacRae, Luuk van der Hoek, Robert van der Wal, Suzanne P. M. de Vette, Hendrike Neh, Baoqiang Ma, Peter M. A. van Ooijen, Lisanne V. van Dijk

Three-dimensional medical image data and computer-aided decision making, particularly using deep learning, are becoming increasingly important in the medical field. To aid in these developments we introduce PR3DICTR: Platform for Research in 3D Image Classification and sTandardised tRaining. Built using community-standard distributions (PyTorch and MONAI), PR3DICTR provides an open-access, flexible and convenient framework for prediction model development, with an explicit focus on classification using three-dimensional medical image data. By combining modular design principles and standardization, it aims to alleviate developmental burden whilst retaining adjustability. It provides users with a wealth of pre-established functionality, for instance in model architecture design options, hyper-parameter solutions and training methodologies, but still gives users the opportunity and freedom to ``plug in'' their own solutions or modules. PR3DICTR can be applied to any binary or event-based three-dimensional classification task and can work with as little as two lines of code.
