##### **TrajOnco: a multi-agent framework for temporal reasoning over longitudinal EHR for multi-cancer early detection**
2604.10386v1 by Sihang Zeng, Young Won Kim, Wilson Lau, Ehsan Alipour, Ruth Etzioni, Meliha Yetisgen, Anand Oka

Accurate estimation of cancer risk from longitudinal electronic health records (EHRs) could support earlier detection and improved care, but modeling such complex patient trajectories remains challenging. We present TrajOnco, a training-free, multi-agent large language model (LLM) framework designed for scalable multi-cancer early detection. Using a chain-of-agents architecture with long-term memory, TrajOnco performs temporal reasoning over sequential clinical events to generate patient-level summaries, evidence-linked rationales, and predicted risk scores. We evaluated TrajOnco on de-identified Truveta EHR data across 15 cancer types using matched case-control cohorts, predicting risk of cancer diagnosis at 1 year. In zero-shot evaluation, TrajOnco achieved AUROCs of 0.64-0.80, performing comparably to supervised machine learning in a lung cancer benchmark while demonstrating better temporal reasoning than single-agent LLMs. The multi-agent design also enabled effective temporal reasoning with smaller-capacity models such as GPT-4.1-mini. The fidelity of TrajOnco's output was validated through human evaluation. Furthermore, TrajOnco's interpretable reasoning outputs can be aggregated to reveal population-level risk patterns that align with established clinical knowledge. These findings highlight the potential of multi-agent LLMs to execute interpretable temporal reasoning over longitudinal EHRs, advancing both scalable multi-cancer early detection and clinical insight generation.

##### **A Diffusion-Contrastive Graph Neural Network with Virtual Nodes for Wind Nowcasting in Unobserved Regions**
2604.10328v1 by Jie Shi, Siamak Mehrkanoon

Accurate weather nowcasting remains one of the central challenges in atmospheric science, with critical implications for climate resilience, energy security, and disaster preparedness. Since it is not feasible to deploy observation stations everywhere, some regions lack dense observational networks, resulting in unreliable short-term wind predictions across those unobserved areas. Here we present a deep graph self-supervised framework that extends nowcasting capability into such unobserved regions without requiring new sensors. Our approach introduces "virtual nodes" into a diffusion and contrastive-based graph neural network, enabling the model to learn wind condition (i.e., speed, direction and gusts) in places with no direct measurements. Using high-temporal resolution weather station data across the Netherlands, we demonstrate that this approach reduces nowcast mean absolute error (MAE) of wind speed, gusts, and direction in unobserved regions by more than 30% - 46% compared with interpolation and regression methods. By enabling localized nowcasts where no measurements exist, this method opens new pathways for renewable energy integration, agricultural planning, and early-warning systems in data-sparse regions.

##### **Jailbreaking the Matrix: Nullspace Steering for Controlled Model Subversion**
2604.10326v1 by Vishal Pramanik, Maisha Maliha, Susmit Jha, Sumit Kumar Jha

Large language models remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks -- inputs designed to bypass safety mechanisms and elicit harmful responses -- despite advances in alignment and instruction tuning. We propose Head-Masked Nullspace Steering (HMNS), a circuit-level intervention that (i) identifies attention heads most causally responsible for a model's default behavior, (ii) suppresses their write paths via targeted column masking, and (iii) injects a perturbation constrained to the orthogonal complement of the muted subspace. HMNS operates in a closed-loop detection-intervention cycle, re-identifying causal heads and reapplying interventions across multiple decoding attempts. Across multiple jailbreak benchmarks, strong safety defenses, and widely used language models, HMNS attains state-of-the-art attack success rates with fewer queries than prior methods. Ablations confirm that nullspace-constrained injection, residual norm scaling, and iterative re-identification are key to its effectiveness. To our knowledge, this is the first jailbreak method to leverage geometry-aware, interpretability-informed interventions, highlighting a new paradigm for controlled model steering and adversarial safety circumvention.

摘要：大型語言模型仍然容易受到越獄攻擊的影響——這些輸入旨在繞過安全機制並引發有害反應——儘管在對齊和指令調整方面有所進展。我們提出了頭部遮罩零空間引導（HMNS），這是一種電路級的干預方法，它 (i) 確定對模型默認行為最具因果責任的注意力頭，(ii) 通過針對性的列遮罩來抑制它們的寫入路徑，以及 (iii) 注入限制在被靜音子空間的正交補空間的擾動。HMNS 在一個閉環檢測-干預循環中運作，重新識別因果頭並在多次解碼嘗試中重新應用干預。在多個越獄基準測試、強大的安全防禦和廣泛使用的語言模型中，HMNS 以比先前方法更少的查詢達到最先進的攻擊成功率。消融實驗確認，受零空間約束的注入、殘差範數縮放和迭代重新識別是其有效性的關鍵。據我們所知，這是第一種利用幾何感知和可解釋性信息的越獄方法，突顯了控制模型引導和對抗安全繞過的新範式。

##### **Gypscie: A Cross-Platform AI Artifact Management System**
2604.10311v1 by Fabio Porto, Eduardo Ogasawara, Gabriela Moraes Botaro, Julia Neumann Bastos, Augusto Fonseca, Esther Pacitti, Patrick Valduriez

Artificial Intelligence (AI) models, encompassing both traditional machine learning (ML) and more advanced approaches such as deep learning and large language models (LLMs), play a central role in modern applications. AI model lifecycle management involves the end-to-end process of managing these models, from data collection and preparation to model building, evaluation, deployment, and continuous monitoring. This process is inherently complex, as it requires the coordination of diverse services that manage AI artifacts such as datasets, dataflows, and models, all orchestrated to operate seamlessly. In this context, it is essential to isolate applications from the complexity of interacting with heterogeneous services, datasets, and AI platforms.
  In this paper, we introduce Gypscie, a cross-platform AI artifact management system. By providing a unified view of all AI artifacts, the Gypscie platform simplifies the development and deployment of AI applications. This unified view is realized through a knowledge graph that captures application semantics and a rule-based query language that supports reasoning over data and models. Model lifecycle activities are represented as high-level dataflows that can be scheduled across multiple platforms, such as servers, cloud platforms, or supercomputers. Finally, Gypscie records provenance information about the artifacts it produces, thereby enabling explainability. Our qualitative comparison with representative AI systems shows that Gypscie supports a broader range of functionalities across the AI artifact lifecycle. Our experimental evaluation demonstrates that Gypscie can successfully optimize and schedule dataflows on AI platforms from an abstract specification.

摘要：人工智慧（AI）模型，包括傳統的機器學習（ML）和更先進的方法，如深度學習和大型語言模型（LLMs），在現代應用中扮演著核心角色。AI模型生命週期管理涉及從數據收集和準備到模型構建、評估、部署和持續監控的端到端過程。這一過程本質上是複雜的，因為它需要協調管理AI工件（如數據集、數據流和模型）的多樣化服務，所有這些服務都被編排以無縫運作。在這個背景下，將應用程序與與異構服務、數據集和AI平台互動的複雜性隔離是至關重要的。<lb/>在本文中，我們介紹了Gypscie，一個跨平台的AI工件管理系統。通過提供所有AI工件的統一視圖，Gypscie平台簡化了AI應用的開發和部署。這一統一視圖是通過捕捉應用語義的知識圖譜和支持對數據和模型進行推理的基於規則的查詢語言實現的。模型生命週期活動被表示為可以在多個平台（如伺服器、雲平台或超級計算機）上調度的高級數據流。最後，Gypscie記錄其生成的工件的來源信息，從而實現可解釋性。我們與代表性AI系統的定性比較顯示，Gypscie在AI工件生命週期中支持更廣泛的功能。我們的實驗評估表明，Gypscie能夠成功地優化和調度AI平台上的數據流，基於抽象規範。

##### **FashionMV: Product-Level Composed Image Retrieval with Multi-View Fashion Data**
2604.10297v1 by Peng Yuan, Bingyin Mei, Hui Zhang

Composed Image Retrieval (CIR) retrieves target images using a reference image paired with modification text. Despite rapid advances, all existing methods and datasets operate at the image level -- a single reference image plus modification text in, a single target image out -- while real e-commerce users reason about products shown from multiple viewpoints. We term this mismatch View Incompleteness and formally define a new Multi-View CIR task that generalizes standard CIR from image-level to product-level retrieval. To support this task, we construct FashionMV, the first large-scale multi-view fashion dataset for product-level CIR, comprising 127K products, 472K multi-view images, and over 220K CIR triplets, built through a fully automated pipeline leveraging large multimodal models. We further propose ProCIR (Product-level Composed Image Retrieval), a modeling framework built upon a multimodal large language model that employs three complementary mechanisms -- two-stage dialogue, caption-based alignment, and chain-of-thought guidance -- together with an optional supervised fine-tuning (SFT) stage that injects structured product knowledge prior to contrastive training. Systematic ablation across 16 configurations on three fashion benchmarks reveals that: (1) alignment is the single most critical mechanism; (2) the two-stage dialogue architecture is a prerequisite for effective alignment; and (3) SFT and chain-of-thought serve as partially redundant knowledge injection paths. Our best 0.8B-parameter model outperforms all baselines, including general-purpose embedding models 10x its size. The dataset, model, and code are publicly available at https://github.com/yuandaxia2001/FashionMV.

摘要：組合圖像檢索（CIR）使用配對的參考圖像和修改文本來檢索目標圖像。儘管快速進步，所有現有的方法和數據集都在圖像層面運作——一個參考圖像加上修改文本輸入，一個目標圖像輸出——而真實的電子商務用戶則從多個視角推理顯示的產品。我們將這種不匹配稱為視圖不完整性，並正式定義一個新的多視圖CIR任務，將標準CIR從圖像層面推廣到產品層面檢索。為了支持這一任務，我們構建了FashionMV，第一個大規模多視圖時尚數據集，用於產品層面CIR，包含127K個產品、472K個多視圖圖像和超過220K個CIR三元組，通過一個完全自動化的管道構建，利用大型多模態模型。我們進一步提出ProCIR（產品層面組合圖像檢索），這是一個基於多模態大型語言模型的建模框架，採用三種互補機制——兩階段對話、基於標題的對齊和思維鏈指導——以及一個可選的監督微調（SFT）階段，該階段在對比訓練之前注入結構化的產品知識。在三個時尚基準上進行的16個配置的系統性消融研究顯示：（1）對齊是最關鍵的單一機制；（2）兩階段對話架構是有效對齊的前提；（3）SFT和思維鏈作為部分冗餘的知識注入路徑。我們最佳的0.8B參數模型超越了所有基準，包括其大小的10倍的通用嵌入模型。數據集、模型和代碼可在https://github.com/yuandaxia2001/FashionMV公開獲得。

##### **The Amazing Agent Race: Strong Tool Users, Weak Navigators**
2604.10261v1 by Zae Myung Kim, Dongseok Lee, Jaehyung Kim, Vipul Raheja, Dongyeop Kang

Existing tool-use benchmarks for LLM agents are overwhelmingly linear: our analysis of six benchmarks shows 55 to 100% of instances are simple chains of 2 to 5 steps. We introduce The Amazing Agent Race (AAR), a benchmark featuring directed acyclic graph (DAG) puzzles (or "legs") with fork-merge tool chains. We release 1,400 instances across two variants: sequential (800 legs) and compositional (600 DAG legs). Agents must navigate Wikipedia, execute multi-step tool chains, and aggregate results into a verifiable answer. Legs are procedurally generated from Wikipedia seeds across four difficulty levels with live-API validation. Three complementary metrics (finish-line accuracy, pit-stop visit rate, and roadblock completion rate) separately diagnose navigation, tool-use, and arithmetic failures. Evaluating three agent frameworks on 1,400 legs, the best achieves only 37.2% accuracy. Navigation errors dominate (27 to 52% of trials) while tool-use errors remain below 17%, and agent architecture matters as much as model scale (Claude Code matches Codex CLI at 37% with 6x fewer tokens). The compositional structure of AAR reveals that agents fail not at calling tools but at navigating to the right pages, a blind spot invisible to linear benchmarks. The project page can be accessed at: https://minnesotanlp.github.io/the-amazing-agent-race

摘要：現有的 LLM 代理工具使用基準大多是線性的：我們對六個基準的分析顯示，55% 到 100% 的實例都是由 2 到 5 步驟組成的簡單鏈。 我們介紹了驚人的代理賽（AAR），這是一個以有向無環圖（DAG）謎題（或稱“腿”）為特色的基準，具有分叉合併的工具鏈。 我們釋出了 1,400 個實例，分為兩個變體：順序（800 腿）和組合（600 DAG 腿）。 代理必須瀏覽維基百科，執行多步驟工具鏈，並將結果匯總成可驗證的答案。 腿是從維基百科種子程序生成的，涵蓋四個難度級別，並進行實時 API 驗證。 三個互補的指標（終點準確性、停靠站訪問率和路障完成率）分別診斷導航、工具使用和算術失敗。 在 1,400 腿上評估三個代理框架，最佳表現僅達到 37.2% 的準確率。 導航錯誤佔主導地位（27% 到 52% 的試驗），而工具使用錯誤則保持在 17% 以下，代理架構的影響與模型規模一樣重要（Claude Code 在 6 倍更少的標記下以 37% 匹配 Codex CLI）。 AAR 的組合結構顯示，代理失敗的並不是呼叫工具，而是導航到正確的頁面，這是線性基準無法察覺的盲點。 項目頁面可以訪問：https://minnesotanlp.github.io/the-amazing-agent-race

##### **CodeComp: Structural KV Cache Compression for Agentic Coding**
2604.10235v1 by Qiujiang Chen, Jing Xiong, Chenyang Zhao, Sidi Yang, Ngai Wong

Agentic code tasks such as fault localization and patch generation require processing long codebases under tight memory constraints, where the Key-Value (KV) cache becomes the primary inference bottleneck. Existing compression methods rely exclusively on attention signals to estimate token importance, systematically discarding structurally critical tokens such as call sites, branch conditions, and assignments that are essential for code understanding. We present CodeComp, a training-free KV cache compression framework that incorporates static program analysis into LLM inference via Code Property Graph priors extracted by Joern. Across bug localization and code generation benchmarks, CodeComp consistently outperforms attention-only compression baselines under equal memory budgets, recovering the majority of full-context accuracy under aggressive KV cache compression, while matching the patch generation quality of uncompressed full-context inference and integrating seamlessly into SGLang-based agentic coding pipelines without model modification.

摘要：代理程式碼任務，例如錯誤定位和補丁生成，需要在嚴格的記憶體限制下處理長代碼庫，其中鍵值（KV）快取成為主要的推理瓶頸。現有的壓縮方法僅依賴於注意力信號來估計標記的重要性，系統性地丟棄結構上關鍵的標記，如調用位置、分支條件和賦值，這些對於代碼理解至關重要。我們提出了 CodeComp，一個無需訓練的 KV 快取壓縮框架，通過 Joern 提取的代碼屬性圖先驗，將靜態程序分析納入 LLM 推理中。在錯誤定位和代碼生成基準測試中，CodeComp 在相同的記憶體預算下持續超越僅基於注意力的壓縮基準，在激進的 KV 快取壓縮下恢復大部分的全上下文準確性，同時匹配未壓縮全上下文推理的補丁生成質量，並無縫整合進基於 SGLang 的代理編碼管道中，無需模型修改。

##### **Relational Probing: LM-to-Graph Adaptation for Financial Prediction**
2604.10212v1 by Yingjie Niu, Changhong Jin, Rian Dolphin, Ruihai Dong

Language models can be used to identify relationships between financial entities in text. However, while structured output mechanisms exist, prompting-based pipelines still incur autoregressive decoding costs and decouple graph construction from downstream optimization. We propose \emph{Relational Probing}, which replaces the standard language-model head with a relation head that induces a relational graph directly from language-model hidden states and is trained jointly with the downstream task model for stock-trend prediction. This approach both learns semantic representations and preserves the strict structure of the induced relational graph. It enables language-model outputs to go beyond text, allowing them to be reshaped into task-specific formats for downstream models. To enhance reproducibility, we provide an operational definition of small language models (SLMs): models that can be fine-tuned end-to-end on a single 24GB GPU under specified batch-size and sequence-length settings. Experiments use Qwen3 backbones (0.6B/1.7B/4B) as upstream SLMs and compare against a co-occurrence baseline. Relational Probing yields consistent performance improvements at competitive inference cost.

摘要：語言模型可以用來識別文本中金融實體之間的關係。<lb/>然而，儘管存在結構化輸出機制，基於提示的管道仍然會產生自回歸解碼成本，並將圖形構建與下游優化解耦。<lb/>我們提出了\emph{關係探測}，它用一個關係頭取代標準的語言模型頭，該關係頭直接從語言模型的隱藏狀態中誘導出一個關係圖，並與下游任務模型共同訓練以進行股票趨勢預測。<lb/>這種方法既學習語義表示，又保留了誘導關係圖的嚴格結構。<lb/>它使語言模型的輸出超越文本，允許它們被重塑為下游模型的任務特定格式。<lb/>為了增強可重現性，我們提供了小型語言模型（SLMs）的操作定義：可以在指定的批次大小和序列長度設置下，在單個24GB GPU上進行端到端微調的模型。<lb/>實驗使用Qwen3骨幹（0.6B/1.7B/4B）作為上游SLMs，並與共現基準進行比較。<lb/>關係探測在具有競爭性推理成本的情況下，產生了一致的性能提升。

##### **FAITH: Factuality Alignment through Integrating Trustworthiness and Honestness**
2604.10189v1 by Xiaoning Dong, Chengyan Wu, Yajie Wen, Yu Chen, Yun Xue, Jing Zhang, Wei Xu, Bolei Ma

Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate factually inaccurate content even if they have corresponding knowledge, which critically undermines their reliability. Existing approaches attempt to mitigate this by incorporating uncertainty in QA prompt during training, but these numerical scores lack the semantic richness for LLM to properly understand its internal states of trustworthiness and honestness, leading to insufficient factuality alignment. We introduce FAITH (Factuality Alignment through Integrating Trustworthiness and Honestness), a post-training framework for factuality alignment that integrates natural-language uncertainty signals with external knowledge. Specifically, we augment training datasets by computing confidence scores and semantic entropy from LLM outputs and mapping them into a knowledge state quadrant that describes the model's internal knowledge possession (trustworthiness) and answering behaviors (honestness) in natural language. Based on this enhanced data, we design a reward function that considers both correctness and uncertainty signals, and fine-tune the LLM using the Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) algorithm. To further mitigate weakly grounded responses, we design a retrieval-augmented module that retrieves relevant external passages, improving the consistency between internal and external knowledge representations. Extensive experiments on four knowledge-intensive benchmarks demonstrate that FAITH enhances the factual accuracy and truthfulness of LLMs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）即使擁有相應的知識，也可能生成事實上不準確的內容，這在根本上削弱了它們的可靠性。現有的方法試圖通過在訓練過程中將不確定性納入問答提示來減輕這一問題，但這些數值分數缺乏語義的豐富性，使得LLM無法正確理解其內部的可信度和誠實度狀態，導致事實對齊不足。我們提出FAITH（通過整合可信度和誠實度實現事實對齊），這是一個用於事實對齊的後訓練框架，整合了自然語言的不確定性信號和外部知識。具體而言，我們通過計算LLM輸出的置信度分數和語義熵，並將其映射到描述模型內部知識擁有（可信度）和回答行為（誠實度）的知識狀態象限來增強訓練數據集。基於這些增強數據，我們設計了一個獎勵函數，考慮到正確性和不確定性信號，並使用近端策略優化（PPO）算法對LLM進行微調。為了進一步減輕弱基礎的回應，我們設計了一個檢索增強模塊，檢索相關的外部段落，提高內部和外部知識表示之間的一致性。在四個知識密集型基準上的大量實驗表明，FAITH增強了LLM的事實準確性和真實性。

##### **MAVEN-T: Multi-Agent enVironment-aware Enhanced Neural Trajectory predictor with Reinforcement Learning**
2604.10169v1 by Wenchang Duan

Trajectory prediction remains a critical yet challenging component in autonomous driving systems, requiring sophisticated reasoning capabilities while meeting strict real-time deployment constraints. While knowledge distillation has demonstrated effectiveness in model compression, existing approaches often fail to preserve complex decision-making capabilities, particularly in dynamic multi-agent scenarios. This paper introduces MAVEN-T, a teacher-student framework that achieves state-of-the-art trajectory prediction through complementary architectural co-design and progressive distillation. The teacher employs hybrid attention mechanisms for maximum representational capacity, while the student uses efficient architectures optimized for deployment. Knowledge transfer is performed via multi-granular distillation with adaptive curriculum learning that dynamically adjusts complexity based on performance. Importantly, the framework incorporates reinforcement learning to overcome the imitation ceiling of traditional distillation, enabling the student to verify, refine, and optimize teacher knowledge through dynamic environmental interaction, potentially achieving more robust decision-making than the teacher itself. Extensive experiments on NGSIM and highD datasets demonstrate 6.2x parameter compression and 3.7x inference speedup while maintaining state-of-the-art accuracy, establishing a new paradigm for deploying sophisticated reasoning models under resource constraints.

摘要：軌跡預測仍然是自動駕駛系統中一個關鍵但具有挑戰性的組成部分，要求具備複雜的推理能力，同時滿足嚴格的實時部署限制。雖然知識蒸餾在模型壓縮方面已顯示出有效性，但現有的方法往往無法保留複雜的決策能力，特別是在動態多代理場景中。本文介紹了MAVEN-T，一個教師-學生框架，通過互補的架構共同設計和漸進式蒸餾實現了最先進的軌跡預測。教師採用混合注意機制以實現最大的表徵能力，而學生則使用為部署優化的高效架構。知識轉移通過多粒度蒸餾進行，並結合自適應課程學習，根據性能動態調整複雜性。重要的是，該框架結合了強化學習，以克服傳統蒸餾的模仿上限，使學生能夠通過動態環境互動驗證、完善和優化教師知識，從而可能實現比教師本身更強健的決策能力。在NGSIM和highD數據集上進行的大規模實驗顯示，參數壓縮達到6.2倍，推理速度提高3.7倍，同時保持最先進的準確性，為在資源限制下部署複雜推理模型建立了一個新範式。

##### **Virtual Smart Metering in District Heating Networks via Heterogeneous Spatial-Temporal Graph Neural Networks**
2604.10166v1 by Keivan Faghih Niresi, Christian Møller Jensen, Carsten Skovmose Kallesøe, Rafael Wisniewski, Olga Fink

Intelligent operation of thermal energy networks aims to improve energy efficiency, reliability, and operational flexibility through data-driven control, predictive optimization, and early fault detection. Achieving these goals relies on sufficient observability, requiring continuous and well-distributed monitoring of thermal and hydraulic states. However, district heating systems are typically sparsely instrumented and frequently affected by sensor faults, limiting monitoring. Virtual sensing offers a cost-effective means to enhance observability, yet its development and validation remain limited in practice. Existing data-driven methods generally assume dense synchronized data, while analytical models rely on simplified hydraulic and thermal assumptions that may not adequately capture the behavior of heterogeneous network topologies. Consequently, modeling the coupled nonlinear dependencies between pressure, flow, and temperature under realistic operating conditions remains challenging. In addition, the lack of publicly available benchmark datasets hinders systematic comparison of virtual sensing approaches. To address these challenges, we propose a heterogeneous spatial-temporal graph neural network (HSTGNN) for constructing virtual smart heat meters. The model incorporates the functional relationships inherent in district heating networks and employs dedicated branches to learn graph structures and temporal dynamics for flow, temperature, and pressure measurements, thereby enabling the joint modeling of cross-variable and spatial correlations. To support further research, we introduce a controlled laboratory dataset collected at the Aalborg Smart Water Infrastructure Laboratory, providing synchronized high-resolution measurements representative of real operating conditions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the proposed approach significantly outperforms existing baselines.

摘要：智能運行熱能網絡旨在通過數據驅動控制、預測優化和早期故障檢測來提高能效、可靠性和運營靈活性。實現這些目標依賴於足夠的可觀測性，這需要對熱和液壓狀態進行持續且良好分佈的監測。然而，區域供熱系統通常儀器稀少，且經常受到傳感器故障的影響，限制了監測。虛擬感測提供了一種成本效益高的方式來增強可觀測性，但其開發和驗證在實踐中仍然有限。現有的數據驅動方法通常假設密集的同步數據，而分析模型則依賴於簡化的液壓和熱假設，這可能無法充分捕捉異質網絡拓撲的行為。因此，在現實操作條件下建模壓力、流量和溫度之間的耦合非線性依賴關係仍然具有挑戰性。此外，缺乏公開可用的基準數據集妨礙了虛擬感測方法的系統比較。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了一種異質時空圖神經網絡（HSTGNN）來構建虛擬智能熱量計。該模型納入了區域供熱網絡固有的功能關係，並利用專門的分支來學習流量、溫度和壓力測量的圖結構和時間動態，從而實現跨變量和空間相關性的聯合建模。為了支持進一步的研究，我們引入了一個在奧爾堡智能水基礎設施實驗室收集的受控實驗室數據集，提供代表真實操作條件的同步高解析度測量。大量實驗表明，所提出的方法顯著優於現有基準。

##### **Inductive Reasoning for Temporal Knowledge Graphs with Emerging Entities**
2604.10164v1 by Ze Zhao, Yuhui He, Lyuwen Wu, Gu Tang, Bin Lu, Xiaoying Gan, Luoyi Fu, Xinbing Wang, Chenghu Zhou

Reasoning on Temporal Knowledge Graphs (TKGs) is essential for predicting future events and time-aware facts. While existing methods are effective at capturing relational dynamics, their performance is limited by a closed-world assumption, which fails to account for emerging entities not present in the training. Notably, these entities continuously join the network without historical interactions. Empirical study reveals that emerging entities are widespread in TKGs, comprising roughly 25\% of all entities. The absence of historical interactions of these entities leads to significant performance degradation in reasoning tasks. Whereas, we observe that entities with semantic similarities often exhibit comparable interaction histories, suggesting the presence of transferable temporal patterns. Inspired by this insight, we propose TransFIR (Transferable Inductive Reasoning), a novel framework that leverages historical interaction sequences from semantically similar known entities to support inductive reasoning. Specifically, we propose a codebook-based classifier that categorizes emerging entities into latent semantic clusters, allowing them to adopt reasoning patterns from similar entities. Experimental results demonstrate that TransFIR outperforms all baselines in reasoning on emerging entities, achieving an average improvement of 28.6% in Mean Reciprocal Rank (MRR) across multiple datasets. The implementations are available at https://github.com/zhaodazhuang2333/TransFIR.

摘要：推理時間知識圖（TKGs）對於預測未來事件和時間感知事實至關重要。雖然現有方法在捕捉關係動態方面有效，但其性能受到封閉世界假設的限制，這無法考慮訓練中未出現的新興實體。值得注意的是，這些實體不斷加入網絡，卻沒有歷史互動。實證研究顯示，新興實體在TKGs中廣泛存在，約佔所有實體的25%。這些實體缺乏歷史互動，導致推理任務中的性能顯著下降。然而，我們觀察到具有語義相似性的實體往往表現出可比的互動歷史，這表明存在可轉移的時間模式。受到這一見解的啟發，我們提出了TransFIR（可轉移的歸納推理），這是一個新穎的框架，利用語義相似的已知實體的歷史互動序列來支持歸納推理。具體而言，我們提出了一種基於碼本的分類器，將新興實體分類到潛在的語義集群中，使它們能夠採用來自相似實體的推理模式。實驗結果表明，TransFIR在對新興實體的推理中超越了所有基準，實現了在多個數據集上平均提高28.6%的平均倒數排名（MRR）。實現可在 https://github.com/zhaodazhuang2333/TransFIR 獲得。

##### **A Temporally Augmented Graph Attention Network for Affordance Classification**
2604.10149v1 by Ami Chopra, Supriya Bordoloi, Shyamanta M. Hazarika

Graph attention networks (GATs) provide one of the best frameworks for learning node representations in relational data; but, existing variants such as Graph Attention Network (GAT) mainly operate on static graphs and rely on implicit temporal aggregation when applied to sequential data. In this paper, we introduce Electroencephalography-temporal Graph Attention Network (EEG-tGAT), a temporally augmented formulation of GATv2 that is tailored for affordance classification from interaction sequences. The proposed model incorporates temporal attention to modulate the contribution of different time segments and temporal dropout to regularize learning across temporally correlated observations. The design reflects the assumption that temporal dimensions in affordance data are not semantically uniform and that discriminative information may be unevenly distributed across time. Experimental results on affordance datasets show that EEG-tGAT achieves improved classification performance compared to GATv2. The observed gains helps to conclude that explicitly encoding temporal importance and enforcing temporal robustness introduce inductive biases that are much better aligned with the structure of affordance-driven interaction data. These findings show us that modest architectural changes to graph attention models can help one obtain consistent benefits when temporal relationships play a nontrivial role in the task.

摘要：圖形注意力網絡（GATs）提供了學習關聯數據中節點表示的最佳框架之一；但是，現有的變體如圖形注意力網絡（GAT）主要在靜態圖上運作，並在應用於序列數據時依賴於隱式的時間聚合。在本文中，我們介紹了腦電圖時間圖形注意力網絡（EEG-tGAT），這是一種針對互動序列的可供性分類量身定制的GATv2的時間增強公式。所提出的模型結合了時間注意力，以調節不同時間段的貢獻，以及時間丟棄以正則化在時間相關觀察中的學習。該設計反映了這樣的假設：可供性數據中的時間維度在語義上並不均勻，且判別信息可能在時間上分佈不均。對可供性數據集的實驗結果顯示，EEG-tGAT相比於GATv2實現了更好的分類性能。觀察到的增益幫助我們得出結論，即明確編碼時間重要性和強化時間穩健性引入的歸納偏差與可供性驅動的互動數據結構更為一致。這些發現告訴我們，對圖形注意力模型進行適度的架構變更可以在時間關係在任務中扮演非平凡角色時，幫助獲得一致的好處。

##### **MR-Coupler: Automated Metamorphic Test Generation via Functional Coupling Analysis**
2604.10126v1 by Congying Xu, Hengcheng Zhu, Songqiang Chen, Jiarong Wu, Valerio Terragni, Shing-Chi Cheung

Metamorphic testing (MT) is a widely recognized technique for alleviating the oracle problem in software testing. However, its adoption is hindered by the difficulty of constructing effective metamorphic relations (MRs), which often require domain-specific or hard-to-obtain knowledge. In this work, we propose a novel approach that leverages the functional coupling between methods, which is readily available in source code, to automatically construct MRs and generate metamorphic test cases (MTCs). Our technique, MR-Coupler, identifies functionally coupled method pairs, employs large language models to generate candidate MTCs, and validates them through test amplification and mutation analysis. In particular, we leverage three functional coupling features to avoid expensive enumeration of possible method pairs, and a novel validation mechanism to reduce false alarms. Our evaluation of MR-Coupler on 100 human-written MTCs and 50 real-world bugs shows that it generates valid MTCs for over 90% of tasks, improves valid MTC generation by 64.90%, and reduces false alarms by 36.56% compared to baselines. Furthermore, the MTCs generated by MR-Coupler detect 44% of the real bugs. Our results highlight the effectiveness of leveraging functional coupling for automated MR construction and the potential of MR-Coupler to facilitate the adoption of MT in practice. We also released the tool and experimental data to support future research.

摘要：變形測試（MT）是一種廣泛認可的技術，用於緩解軟體測試中的神諭問題。<lb/>然而，其採用受到構建有效變形關係（MRs）難度的阻礙，這通常需要特定領域或難以獲得的知識。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了一種新穎的方法，利用源代碼中可用的功能耦合來自動構建MRs並生成變形測試案例（MTCs）。<lb/>我們的技術MR-Coupler識別功能耦合的函數對，利用大型語言模型生成候選MTCs，並通過測試擴增和突變分析進行驗證。<lb/>特別是，我們利用三個功能耦合特徵來避免昂貴的可能函數對的枚舉，以及一種新穎的驗證機制來減少誤報。<lb/>我們對MR-Coupler在100個人類編寫的MTCs和50個真實世界錯誤的評估顯示，它為超過90%的任務生成有效的MTCs，並將有效MTC生成提高了64.90%，與基準相比，減少了36.56%的誤報。<lb/>此外，MR-Coupler生成的MTCs檢測到44%的真實錯誤。<lb/>我們的結果突顯了利用功能耦合進行自動MR構建的有效性，以及MR-Coupler促進MT在實踐中採用的潛力。<lb/>我們還發布了該工具和實驗數據以支持未來的研究。

##### **A Dual Cross-Attention Graph Learning Framework For Multimodal MRI-Based Major Depressive Disorder Detection**
2604.10116v1 by Nojod M. Alotaibi, Areej M. Alhothali

Major depressive disorder (MDD) is a prevalent mental disorder associated with complex neurobiological changes that cannot be fully captured using a single imaging modality. The use of multimodal magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) provides a more comprehensive understanding of brain changes by combining structural and functional data. Despite this, the effective integration of these modalities remains challenging. In this study, we propose a dual cross-attention-based multimodal fusion framework that explicitly models bidirectional interactions between structural MRI (sMRI) and resting-state functional MRI (rs-fMRI) representations. The proposed approach is tested on the large-scale REST-meta-MDD dataset using both structural and functional brain atlas configurations. Numerous experiments conducted under a 10-fold stratified cross-validation demonstrated that the proposed fusion algorithm achieves robust and competitive performance across all atlas types. The proposed method consistently outperforms conventional feature-level concatenation for functional atlases, while maintaining comparable performance for structural atlases. The most effective dual cross-attention multimodal model obtained 84.71% accuracy, 86.42% sensitivity, 82.89% specificity, 84.34% precision, and 85.37% F1-score. These findings emphasize the importance of explicitly modeling cross-modal interactions for multimodal neuroimaging-based MDD classification.

摘要：重度憂鬱症（MDD）是一種普遍的心理疾病，與複雜的神經生物學變化相關，這些變化無法僅通過單一成像模式完全捕捉。使用多模態磁共振成像（MRI）通過結合結構性和功能性數據提供了對大腦變化的更全面理解。儘管如此，這些模態的有效整合仍然具有挑戰性。在本研究中，我們提出了一種基於雙重交叉注意力的多模態融合框架，明確建模結構性MRI（sMRI）和靜息態功能性MRI（rs-fMRI）表示之間的雙向互動。所提出的方法在大型REST-meta-MDD數據集上進行測試，使用結構性和功能性大腦圖譜配置。在10折分層交叉驗證下進行的多項實驗表明，所提出的融合算法在所有圖譜類型中都達到了穩健且具有競爭力的性能。所提出的方法在功能性圖譜上始終優於傳統的特徵級串聯，同時在結構性圖譜上保持可比的性能。最有效的雙重交叉注意力多模態模型達到了84.71%的準確率、86.42%的敏感性、82.89%的特異性、84.34%的精確率和85.37%的F1分數。這些發現強調了明確建模跨模態互動在基於多模態神經成像的MDD分類中的重要性。

##### **Ontological Trajectory Forecasting via Finite Semigroup Iteration and Lie Algebra Approximation in Geopolitical Knowledge Graphs**
2604.10087v1 by Qihang Wu

We present EL-DRUIN, an ontological reasoning system for geopolitical intelligence analysis that combines formal ontology, finite semigroup algebra, and Lie algebra approximation to forecast long-run relationship trajectories. Current LLM-based political analysis systems operate as summarisation engines, producing outputs bounded by textual pattern matching. EL-DRUIN departs from this paradigm by modelling geopolitical relationships as states in a finite set of named Dynamic Patterns, composing patterns via a semigroup operation whose structure constants are defined by an explicit composition table, and embedding each pattern as a vector in an 8-dimensional semantic Lie algebra space. Forward simulation iterates this semigroup operation, yielding reachable pattern sets at each discrete timestep; convergence to idempotent absorbing states (fixed points of the composition) constitutes the predicted long-run attractor. Bayesian posterior weights combine ontology-derived confidence priors with a Lie similarity term measuring the cosine similarity between the vector sum of composing patterns and the target pattern vector, providing interpretable, calibrated probabilities that are not self-reported by a language model. Bifurcation points -- steps at which two candidate attractors have near-equal posterior mass -- are detected and exposed to downstream analysis. We demonstrate the framework on six geopolitical scenarios including US-China technology decoupling and the Taiwan Strait military coercion trajectory. The architecture is publicly available as an open-source system with a Streamlit frontend exposing full computation traces, Bayesian posterior breakdowns, and 8D ontological state vectors.

摘要：我們提出了EL-DRUIN，一個用於地緣政治情報分析的本體推理系統，結合了形式本體、有限半群代數和李代數近似，以預測長期關係軌跡。當前基於LLM的政治分析系統作為摘要引擎運作，產生的輸出受限於文本模式匹配。EL-DRUIN脫離了這一範式，將地緣政治關係建模為有限集合中的命名動態模式的狀態，通過一個結構常數由明確組合表定義的半群運算來組合模式，並將每個模式嵌入到一個8維語義李代數空間中。前向模擬重複這個半群運算，在每個離散時間步產生可達的模式集；收斂到冪等吸收狀態（組合的固定點）構成了預測的長期吸引子。貝葉斯後驗權重結合了本體推導的置信先驗和測量組合模式的向量和與目標模式向量之間餘弦相似性的李相似性項，提供可解釋的、經過校準的概率，這些概率並不是由語言模型自我報告的。分岔點——兩個候選吸引子具有近乎相等的後驗質量的步驟——被檢測並暴露於下游分析。我們在六個地緣政治情境中展示了該框架，包括美中技術脫鉤和台灣海峽軍事脅迫軌跡。該架構作為開源系統公開可用，具有Streamlit前端，顯示完整的計算痕跡、貝葉斯後驗分解和8D本體狀態向量。

##### **Why Supervised Fine-Tuning Fails to Learn: A Systematic Study of Incomplete Learning in Large Language Models**
2604.10079v1 by Chao Xue, Yao Wang, Mengqiao Liu, Di Liang, Xingsheng Han, Peiyang Liu, Xianjie Wu, Chenyao Lu, Lei Jiang, Yu Lu, Haibo Shi, Shuang Liang, Minlong Peng, Flora D. Salim

Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) is the standard approach for adapting large language models (LLMs) to downstream tasks. However, we observe a persistent failure mode: even after convergence, models often fail to correctly reproduce a subset of their own supervised training data. We refer to this behavior as the Incomplete Learning Phenomenon(ILP). This paper presents the first systematic study of ILP in LLM fine-tuning. We formalize ILP as post-training failure to internalize supervised instances and demonstrate its prevalence across multiple model families, domains, and datasets. Through controlled analyses, we identify five recurrent sources of incomplete learning: (1) missing prerequisite knowledge in the pre-trained model, (2) conflicts between SFT supervision and pre-training knowledge, (3) internal inconsistencies within SFT data, (4) left-side forgetting during sequential fine-tuning, and (5) insufficient optimization for rare or complex patterns. We introduce a diagnostic-first framework that maps unlearned samples to these causes using observable training and inference signals, and study several targeted mitigation strategies as causal interventions. Experiments on Qwen, LLaMA, and OLMo2 show that incomplete learning is widespread and heterogeneous, and that improvements in aggregate metrics can mask persistent unlearned subsets. The findings highlight the need for fine-grained diagnosis of what supervised fine-tuning fails to learn, and why.

摘要：監督微調（SFT）是將大型語言模型（LLMs）適應於下游任務的標準方法。<lb/>然而，我們觀察到一種持續的失敗模式：即使在收斂後，模型經常無法正確重現其自身監督訓練數據的一部分。<lb/>我們將這種行為稱為不完全學習現象（ILP）。<lb/>本文呈現了對LLM微調中ILP的首次系統研究。<lb/>我們將ILP形式化為在訓練後未能內化監督實例，並展示其在多個模型家族、領域和數據集中的普遍性。<lb/>通過控制分析，我們識別出五個不完全學習的重複來源：（1）預訓練模型中缺失的先決知識，（2）SFT監督與預訓練知識之間的衝突，（3）SFT數據內部的不一致性，（4）在序列微調過程中的左側遺忘，以及（5）對稀有或複雜模式的優化不足。<lb/>我們引入了一個以診斷為先的框架，將未學習的樣本映射到這些原因，使用可觀察的訓練和推斷信號，並研究幾種針對性的緩解策略作為因果干預。<lb/>在Qwen、LLaMA和OLMo2上的實驗顯示，不完全學習是普遍且異質的，並且整體指標的改善可能掩蓋持續存在的未學習子集。<lb/>這些發現凸顯了對監督微調未能學習的內容及其原因進行細緻診斷的必要性。

##### **Learning Hierarchical and Geometry-Aware Graph Representations for Text-to-CAD**
2604.10075v1 by Shengjie Gong, Wenjie Peng, Hongyuan Chen, Gangyu Zhang, Yunqing Hu, Huiyuan Zhang, Shuangping Huang, Tianshui Chen

Text-to-CAD code generation is a long-horizon task that translates textual instructions into long sequences of interdependent operations. Existing methods typically decode text directly into executable code (e.g., bpy) without explicitly modeling assembly hierarchy or geometric constraints, which enlarges the search space, accumulates local errors, and often causes cascading failures in complex assemblies. To address this issue, we propose a hierarchical and geometry-aware graph as an intermediate representation. The graph models multi-level parts and components as nodes and encodes explicit geometric constraints as edges. Instead of mapping text directly to code, our framework first predicts structure and constraints, then conditions action sequencing and code generation, thereby improving geometric fidelity and constraint satisfaction. We further introduce a structure-aware progressive curriculum learning strategy that constructs graded tasks through controlled structural edits, explores the model's capability boundary, and synthesizes boundary examples for iterative training. In addition, we build a 12K dataset with instructions, decomposition graphs, action sequences, and bpy code, together with graph- and constraint-oriented evaluation metrics. Extensive experiments show that our method consistently outperforms existing approaches in both geometric fidelity and accurate satisfaction of geometric constraints.

摘要：文本到CAD代碼生成是一項長期任務，將文本指令轉換為長序列的相互依賴操作。現有的方法通常將文本直接解碼為可執行代碼（例如，bpy），而不明確建模組裝層次或幾何約束，這擴大了搜索空間，積累了局部錯誤，並且常常導致複雜組裝中的連鎖故障。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了一種分層和幾何感知圖作為中介表示。該圖將多層次的零件和組件建模為節點，並將明確的幾何約束編碼為邊。與其將文本直接映射到代碼，我們的框架首先預測結構和約束，然後條件化行動序列和代碼生成，從而提高幾何真實性和約束滿足度。我們進一步引入了一種結構感知的漸進課程學習策略，通過受控的結構編輯構建分級任務，探索模型的能力邊界，並合成邊界示例以進行迭代訓練。此外，我們建立了一個包含指令、分解圖、行動序列和bpy代碼的12K數據集，以及面向圖和約束的評估指標。大量實驗表明，我們的方法在幾何真實性和準確滿足幾何約束方面始終優於現有方法。

##### **Graph-RHO: Critical-path-aware Heterogeneous Graph Network for Long-Horizon Flexible Job-Shop Scheduling**
2604.10073v1 by Yujie Li, Jiuniu Wang, Mugen Peng, Guangzuo Li, Wenjia Xu

Long-horizon Flexible Job-Shop Scheduling~(FJSP) presents a formidable combinatorial challenge due to complex, interdependent decisions spanning extended time horizons. While learning-based Rolling Horizon Optimization~(RHO) has emerged as a promising paradigm to accelerate solving by identifying and fixing invariant operations, its effectiveness is hindered by the structural complexity of FJSP. Existing methods often fail to capture intricate graph-structured dependencies and ignore the asymmetric costs of prediction errors, in which misclassifying critical-path operations is significantly more detrimental than misclassifying non-critical ones. Furthermore, dynamic shifts in predictive confidence during the rolling process make static pruning thresholds inadequate. To address these limitations, we propose Graph-RHO, a novel critical-path-aware graph-based RHO framework. First, we introduce a topology-aware heterogeneous graph network that encodes subproblems as operation-machine graphs with multi-relational edges, leveraging edge-feature-aware message passing to predict operation stability. Second, we incorporate a critical-path-aware mechanism that injects inductive biases during training to distinguish highly sensitive bottleneck operations from robust ones. Third, we devise an adaptive thresholding strategy that dynamically calibrates decision boundaries based on online uncertainty estimation to align model predictions with the solver's search space. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that \mbox{Graph-RHO} establishes a new state of the art in solution quality and computational efficiency. Remarkably, it exhibits exceptional zero-shot generalization, reducing solve time by over 30\% on large-scale instances (2000 operations) while achieving superior solution quality. Our code is available \href{https://github.com/IntelliSensing/Graph-RHO}{here}.

摘要：長期靈活工作車間排程（FJSP）因為複雜且相互依賴的決策跨越長時間範圍而呈現出可怕的組合挑戰。雖然基於學習的滾動視野優化（RHO）已成為一種有前景的範式，通過識別和修正不變操作來加速求解，但其有效性受到FJSP結構複雜性的阻礙。現有方法往往無法捕捉複雜的圖結構依賴關係，並忽略預測錯誤的非對稱成本，其中錯誤分類關鍵路徑操作的損害遠大於錯誤分類非關鍵操作的損害。此外，在滾動過程中預測信心的動態變化使得靜態修剪閾值不再適用。為了應對這些限制，我們提出了Graph-RHO，一種新穎的關鍵路徑感知圖基RHO框架。首先，我們引入了一種拓撲感知的異質圖網絡，將子問題編碼為具有多關係邊的操作-機器圖，利用邊特徵感知的消息傳遞來預測操作穩定性。其次，我們納入了一種關鍵路徑感知機制，在訓練過程中注入歸納偏見，以區分高度敏感的瓶頸操作與穩健操作。第三，我們設計了一種自適應閾值策略，根據在線不確定性估計動態校準決策邊界，以使模型預測與求解器的搜索空間對齊。在標準基準上的廣泛實驗表明，\mbox{Graph-RHO}在解決方案質量和計算效率方面建立了新的最先進水平。值得注意的是，它展現出卓越的零-shot泛化能力，在大規模實例（2000個操作）上將求解時間減少超過30\%，同時實現了更優的解決方案質量。我們的代碼可以在\href{https://github.com/IntelliSensing/Graph-RHO}{這裡}獲得。

##### **CoSToM:Causal-oriented Steering for Intrinsic Theory-of-Mind Alignment in Large Language Models**
2604.10031v1 by Mengfan Li, Xuanhua Shi, Yang Deng

Theory of Mind (ToM), the ability to attribute mental states to others, is a hallmark of social intelligence. While large language models (LLMs) demonstrate promising performance on standard ToM benchmarks, we observe that they often fail to generalize to complex task-specific scenarios, relying heavily on prompt scaffolding to mimic reasoning. The critical misalignment between the internal knowledge and external behavior raises a fundamental question: Do LLMs truly possess intrinsic cognition, and can they externalize this internal knowledge into stable, high-quality behaviors? To answer this, we introduce CoSToM (Causal-oriented Steering for ToM alignment), a framework that transitions from mechanistic interpretation to active intervention. First, we employ causal tracing to map the internal distribution of ToM features, empirically uncovering the internal layers' characteristics in encoding fundamental ToM semantics. Building on this insight, we implement a lightweight alignment framework via targeted activation steering within these ToM-critical layers. Experiments demonstrate that CoSToM significantly enhances human-like social reasoning capabilities and downstream dialogue quality.

##### **New Hybrid Fine-Tuning Paradigm for LLMs: Algorithm Design and Convergence Analysis Framework**
2604.09940v1 by Shaocong Ma, Peiran Yu, Heng Huang

Fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) typically involves either full fine-tuning, which updates all model parameters, or Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT), which adjusts a small subset of parameters. However, both approaches have inherent limitations: full fine-tuning is computationally expensive, while PEFT often struggles to learn new knowledge and exhibits suboptimal performance. To overcome these issues, we propose a novel hybrid fine-tuning approach that jointly updates both LLMs and PEFT modules using a combination of zeroth-order and first-order optimization methods. To analyze our new algorithm, we develop a theoretical framework centered on the concept of hybrid smoothness condition, which accounts for the heterogeneous nature of the optimization landscape in joint LLM and PEFT training. We derive a rigorous convergence analysis for the convergence of reshuffling-type SGD algorithm under multiple learning rates and demonstrate its effectiveness through extensive empirical studies across various downstream tasks and model architectures. On the practical side, our results demonstrate consistent performance improvement, making the approach a viable solution for large-scale language model fine-tuning.

摘要：微調大型語言模型（LLMs）通常涉及完全微調，這會更新所有模型參數，或是參數高效微調（PEFT），這會調整一小部分參數。<lb/>然而，這兩種方法都有固有的限制：完全微調計算成本高，而PEFT則常常難以學習新知識並表現不佳。<lb/>為了解決這些問題，我們提出了一種新穎的混合微調方法，該方法使用零階和一階優化方法的結合，聯合更新LLMs和PEFT模組。<lb/>為了分析我們的新算法，我們開發了一個以混合平滑條件為中心的理論框架，該框架考慮了聯合LLM和PEFT訓練中優化景觀的異質性。<lb/>我們推導了在多個學習率下重排型SGD算法的收斂分析，並通過在各種下游任務和模型架構中的廣泛實證研究證明了其有效性。<lb/>在實踐方面，我們的結果顯示出穩定的性能提升，使該方法成為大規模語言模型微調的可行解決方案。

##### **From UAV Imagery to Agronomic Reasoning: A Multimodal LLM Benchmark for Plant Phenotyping**
2604.09907v1 by Yu Wu, Guangzeng Han, Ibra Niang Niang, Francia Ravelombola, Maiara Oliveira, Jason Davis, Dong Chen, Feng Lin, Xiaolei Huang

To improve crop genetics, high-throughput, effective and comprehensive phenotyping is a critical prerequisite. While such tasks were traditionally performed manually, recent advances in multimodal foundation models, especially in vision-language models (VLMs), have enabled more automated and robust phenotypic analysis. However, plant science remains a particularly challenging domain for foundation models because it requires domain-specific knowledge, fine-grained visual interpretation, and complex biological and agronomic reasoning. To address this gap, we develop PlantXpert, an evidence-grounded multimodal reasoning benchmark for soybean and cotton phenotyping. Our benchmark provides a structured and reproducible framework for agronomic adaptation of VLMs, and enables controlled comparison between base models and their domain-adapted counterparts. We constructed a dataset comprising 385 digital images and more than 3,000 benchmark samples spanning key plant science domains including disease, pest control, weed management, and yield. The benchmark can assess diverse capabilities including visual expertise, quantitative reasoning, and multi-step agronomic reasoning. A total of 11 state-of-the-art VLMs were evaluated. The results indicate that task-specific fine-tuning leads to substantial improvement in accuracy, with models such as Qwen3-VL-4B and Qwen3-VL-30B achieving up to 78%. At the same time, gains from model scaling diminish beyond a certain capacity, generalization across soybean and cotton remains uneven, and quantitative as well as biologically grounded reasoning continue to pose substantial challenges. These findings suggest that PlantXpert can serve as a foundation for assessing evidence-grounded agronomic reasoning and for advancing multimodal model development in plant science.

摘要：為了改善作物基因，進行高通量、有效且全面的表型分析是關鍵的前提條件。雖然這些任務傳統上是手動執行的，但最近在多模態基礎模型方面的進展，特別是在視覺-語言模型（VLMs）中，使得更自動化和穩健的表型分析成為可能。然而，植物科學對於基礎模型來說仍然是一個特別具有挑戰性的領域，因為它需要特定領域的知識、細緻的視覺解釋以及複雜的生物和農業推理。為了解決這一差距，我們開發了PlantXpert，一個以證據為基礎的多模態推理基準，專注於大豆和棉花的表型分析。我們的基準提供了一個結構化和可重複的框架，用於VLM的農業適應，並使基礎模型與其領域適應版本之間的控制比較成為可能。我們構建了一個數據集，包含385張數字圖像和超過3,000個基準樣本，涵蓋了包括疾病、害蟲控制、雜草管理和產量等關鍵植物科學領域。該基準可以評估多種能力，包括視覺專業知識、定量推理和多步驟農業推理。共評估了11個最先進的VLM。結果顯示，針對特定任務的微調會顯著提高準確性，像Qwen3-VL-4B和Qwen3-VL-30B等模型的準確率高達78%。同時，模型擴展所帶來的增益在達到某一容量後會減少，對於大豆和棉花的泛化仍然不均勻，定量以及生物學基礎的推理仍然面臨重大挑戰。這些發現表明，PlantXpert可以作為評估以證據為基礎的農業推理的基礎，並推進植物科學中多模態模型的發展。

##### **Not Your Stereo-Typical Estimator: Combining Vision and Language for Volume Perception**
2604.09886v1 by Gautham Vinod, Bruce Coburn, Siddeshwar Raghavan, Fengqing Zhu

Accurate volume estimation of objects from visual data is a long-standing challenge in computer vision with significant applications in robotics, logistics, and smart health. Existing methods often rely on complex 3D reconstruction pipelines or struggle with the ambiguity inherent in single-view images. To address these limitations, we introduce a new method that fuses implicit 3D cues from stereo vision with explicit prior knowledge from natural language text. Our approach extracts deep features from a stereo image pair and a descriptive text prompt that contains the object's class and an approximate volume, then integrates them using a simple yet effective projection layer into a unified, multi-modal representation for regression. We conduct extensive experiments on public datasets demonstrating that our text-guided approach significantly outperforms vision-only baselines. Our findings show that leveraging even simple textual priors can effectively guide the volume estimation task, paving the way for more context-aware visual measurement systems. Code: https://gitlab.com/viper-purdue/stereo-typical-estimator.

摘要：從視覺數據準確估算物體體積一直是計算機視覺中的一個長期挑戰，並在機器人技術、物流和智能健康等領域具有重要應用。現有的方法通常依賴於複雜的三維重建流程，或者在單視圖圖像中掙扎於固有的模糊性。為了解決這些限制，我們提出了一種新方法，將來自立體視覺的隱含三維線索與來自自然語言文本的明確先驗知識相融合。我們的方法從一對立體圖像和包含物體類別及近似體積的描述性文本提示中提取深層特徵，然後使用一個簡單而有效的投影層將它們整合成統一的多模態表示以進行回歸。我們在公共數據集上進行了廣泛的實驗，證明我們的文本引導方法顯著超越了僅依賴視覺的基準。我們的研究結果顯示，即使是利用簡單的文本先驗也能有效指導體積估算任務，為更具上下文感知的視覺測量系統鋪平道路。代碼：https://gitlab.com/viper-purdue/stereo-typical-estimator。

##### **Simulating Organized Group Behavior: New Framework, Benchmark, and Analysis**
2604.09874v1 by Xinkai Zou, Yiming Huang, Zhuohang Wu, Jian Sha, Nan Huang, Longfei Yun, Jingbo Shang, Letian Peng

Simulating how organized groups (e.g., corporations) make decisions (e.g., responding to a competitor's move) is essential for understanding real-world dynamics and could benefit relevant applications (e.g., market prediction). In this paper, we formalize this problem as a concrete research platform for group behavior understanding, providing: (1) a task definition with benchmark and evaluation criteria, (2) a structured analytical framework with a corresponding algorithm, and (3) detailed temporal and cross-group analysis. Specifically, we propose Organized Group Behavior Simulation, a task that models organized groups as collective entities from a practical perspective: given a group facing a particular situation (e.g., AI Boom), predict the decision it would take. To support this task, we present GROVE (GRoup Organizational BehaVior Evaluation), a benchmark covering 44 entities with 8,052 real-world context-decision pairs collected from Wikipedia and TechCrunch across 9 domains, with an end-to-end evaluation protocol assessing consistency, initiative, scope, magnitude, and horizon. Beyond straightforward prompting pipelines, we propose a structured analytical framework that converts collective decision-making events into an interpretable, adaptive, and traceable behavioral model, achieving stronger performance than summarization- and retrieval-based baselines. It further introduces an adapter mechanism for time-aware evolution and group-aware transfer, and traceable evidence nodes grounding each decision rule in originating historical events. Our analysis reveals temporal behavioral drift within individual groups, which the time-aware adapter effectively captures for stronger prediction, and structured cross-group similarity that enables knowledge transfer for data-scarce organizations.

摘要：模擬有組織的團體（例如，企業）如何做出決策（例如，對競爭對手的行動作出反應）對於理解現實世界的動態至關重要，並可能對相關應用（例如，市場預測）帶來好處。本文將此問題形式化為一個具體的研究平台，以理解團體行為，提供：（1）具有基準和評估標準的任務定義，（2）具有相應算法的結構化分析框架，以及（3）詳細的時間和跨團體分析。具體而言，我們提出有組織的團體行為模擬，這是一項從實際角度建模有組織團體作為集體實體的任務：給定一個面對特定情況（例如，人工智慧熱潮）的團體，預測它將採取的決策。為了支持這項任務，我們提出了GROVE（GRoup Organizational BehaVior Evaluation），這是一個基準，涵蓋44個實體，並從Wikipedia和TechCrunch收集了8,052對現實世界的上下文-決策對，跨越9個領域，並具有端到端的評估協議，評估一致性、主動性、範疇、規模和視野。除了簡單的提示管道外，我們還提出了一個結構化的分析框架，將集體決策事件轉換為可解釋的、自適應的和可追溯的行為模型，實現比基於摘要和檢索的基準更強的性能。它進一步引入了一個適配器機制，用於時間感知的演變和團體感知的轉移，以及可追溯的證據節點，將每個決策規則與源自的歷史事件相連接。我們的分析揭示了個別團體內的時間行為漂移，時間感知的適配器有效捕捉了這一點，以實現更強的預測，並且結構化的跨團體相似性使數據稀缺的組織能夠進行知識轉移。

##### **Is There Knowledge Left to Extract? Evidence of Fragility in Medically Fine-Tuned Vision-Language Models**
2604.09841v1 by Oliver McLaughlin, Daniel Shubin, Carsten Eickhoff, Ritambhara Singh, William Rudman, Michal Golovanevsky

Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly adapted through domain-specific fine-tuning, yet it remains unclear whether this improves reasoning beyond superficial visual cues, particularly in high-stakes domains like medicine. We evaluate four paired open-source VLMs (LLaVA vs. LLaVA-Med; Gemma vs. MedGemma) across four medical imaging tasks of increasing difficulty: brain tumor, pneumonia, skin cancer, and histopathology classification. We find that performance degrades toward near-random levels as task difficulty increases, indicating limited clinical reasoning. Medical fine-tuning provides no consistent advantage, and models are highly sensitive to prompt formulation, with minor changes causing large swings in accuracy and refusal rates. To test whether closed-form VQA suppresses latent knowledge, we introduce a description-based pipeline where models generate image descriptions that a text-only model (GPT-5.1) uses for diagnosis. This recovers a limited additional signal but remains bounded by task difficulty. Analysis of vision encoder embeddings further shows that failures stem from both weak visual representations and downstream reasoning. Overall, medical VLM performance is fragile, prompt-dependent, and not reliably improved by domain-specific fine-tuning.

摘要：視覺-語言模型（VLMs）越來越多地通過特定領域的微調進行調整，但尚不清楚這是否能改善推理能力，超越表面的視覺線索，特別是在像醫學這樣的高風險領域。我們評估了四對開源VLM（LLaVA與LLaVA-Med；Gemma與MedGemma）在四個逐漸增加難度的醫學影像任務中的表現：腦腫瘤、肺炎、皮膚癌和組織病理學分類。我們發現，隨著任務難度的增加，表現會降至接近隨機的水平，這表明臨床推理能力有限。醫學微調並未提供一致的優勢，模型對提示的表述高度敏感，輕微的變化會導致準確率和拒絕率的大幅波動。為了測試封閉形式的VQA是否抑制潛在知識，我們引入了一個基於描述的流程，模型生成的圖像描述供一個僅文本模型（GPT-5.1）用於診斷。這恢復了一定的額外信號，但仍然受到任務難度的限制。對視覺編碼器嵌入的分析進一步顯示，失敗源於弱視覺表徵和下游推理的問題。總體而言，醫學VLM的表現脆弱，依賴於提示，並且不會因特定領域的微調而可靠地改善。

##### **ProGAL-VLA: Grounded Alignment through Prospective Reasoning in Vision-Language-Action Models**
2604.09824v1 by Nastaran Darabi, Amit Ranjan Trivedi

Vision language action (VLA) models enable generalist robotic agents but often exhibit language ignorance, relying on visual shortcuts and remaining insensitive to instruction changes. We present Prospective Grounding and Alignment VLA (ProGAL-VLA), which constructs a 3D entity-centric graph (GSM), uses a slow planner to produce symbolic sub-goals, and aligns them with grounded entities via a Grounding Alignment Contrastive (GAC) loss. All actions are conditioned on a verified goal embedding $g_t$, whose attention entropy provides an intrinsic ambiguity signal. On LIBERO-Plus, ProGAL-VLA increases robustness under robot perturbations from 30.3 to 71.5 percent, reduces language ignorance by 3x-4x, and improves entity retrieval from 0.41 to 0.71 Recall@1. On the Custom Ambiguity Benchmark, it reaches AUROC 0.81 (vs. 0.52), AUPR 0.79, and raises clarification on ambiguous inputs from 0.09 to 0.81 without harming unambiguous success. The verification bottleneck increases mutual information of language-actions, the GAC loss imposes an entity-level InfoNCE bound, and attention entropy yields calibrated selective prediction, indicating that explicit verified grounding is an effective path toward instruction-sensitive, ambiguity-aware agents.

摘要：視覺語言行動 (VLA) 模型使通用機器人代理成為可能，但常常表現出語言無知，依賴視覺捷徑，並對指令變更保持不敏感。我們提出了前瞻性基礎和對齊 VLA (ProGAL-VLA)，該模型構建了一個以 3D 實體為中心的圖 (GSM)，使用慢速規劃器生成符號子目標，並通過基礎對齊對比 (GAC) 損失將其與基礎實體對齊。所有行動都以經過驗證的目標嵌入 $g_t$ 為條件，其注意力熵提供了一個內在的模糊信號。在 LIBERO-Plus 上，ProGAL-VLA 在機器人擾動下的穩健性從 30.3% 提高到 71.5%，語言無知減少了 3 倍至 4 倍，實體檢索從 0.41 提高到 0.71 Recall@1。在自定義模糊基準上，它達到 AUROC 0.81 (對比 0.52)，AUPR 0.79，並將對模糊輸入的澄清從 0.09 提高到 0.81，而不損害明確成功。驗證瓶頸增加了語言-行動的互信息，GAC 損失施加了實體級別的 InfoNCE 界限，注意力熵產生了經過校準的選擇性預測，這表明明確的驗證基礎是朝向對指令敏感、意識到模糊的代理的有效途徑。

##### **Claim2Vec: Embedding Fact-Check Claims for Multilingual Similarity and Clustering**
2604.09812v1 by Rrubaa Panchendrarajan, Arkaitz Zubiaga

Recurrent claims present a major challenge for automated fact-checking systems designed to combat misinformation, especially in multilingual settings. While tasks such as claim matching and fact-checked claim retrieval aim to address this problem by linking claim pairs, the broader challenge of effectively representing groups of similar claims that can be resolved with the same fact-check via claim clustering remains relatively underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce Claim2Vec, the first multilingual embedding model optimized to represent fact-check claims as vectors in an improved semantic embedding space. We fine-tune a multilingual encoder using contrastive learning with similar multilingual claim pairs. Experiments on the claim clustering task using three datasets, 14 multilingual embedding models, and 7 clustering algorithms demonstrate that Claim2Vec significantly improves clustering performance. Specifically, it enhances both cluster label alignment and the geometric structure of the embedding space across different cluster configurations. Our multilingual analysis shows that clusters containing multiple languages benefit from fine-tuning, demonstrating cross-lingual knowledge transfer.

摘要：重複的主張對於旨在打擊錯誤資訊的自動事實查核系統構成了重大挑戰，尤其是在多語言環境中。<lb/>雖然主張匹配和事實查核主張檢索等任務旨在通過連結主張對來解決這個問題，但有效表示可以通過主張聚類以相同事實查核解決的相似主張群體的更廣泛挑戰仍然相對未被充分探討。<lb/>為了解決這個空白，我們介紹了Claim2Vec，這是第一個優化以向量形式表示事實查核主張的多語言嵌入模型，並在改進的語義嵌入空間中進行表示。<lb/>我們使用對比學習對相似的多語言主張對進行微調，從而微調一個多語言編碼器。<lb/>在使用三個數據集、14個多語言嵌入模型和7個聚類算法的主張聚類任務上的實驗表明，Claim2Vec顯著改善了聚類性能。<lb/>具體而言，它增強了不同聚類配置中聚類標籤對齊和嵌入空間的幾何結構。<lb/>我們的多語言分析顯示，包含多種語言的聚類受益於微調，顯示出跨語言知識轉移的效果。

##### **XFED: Non-Collusive Model Poisoning Attack Against Byzantine-Robust Federated Classifiers**
2604.09489v1 by Israt Jahan Mouri, Muhammad Ridowan, Muhammad Abdullah Adnan

Model poisoning attacks pose a significant security threat to Federated Learning (FL). Most existing model poisoning attacks rely on collusion, requiring adversarial clients to coordinate by exchanging local benign models and synchronizing the generation of their poisoned updates. However, sustaining such coordination is increasingly impractical in real-world FL deployments, as it effectively requires botnet-like control over many devices. This approach is costly to maintain and highly vulnerable to detection. This context raises a fundamental question: Can model poisoning attacks remain effective without any communication between attackers? To address this challenge, we introduce and formalize the \textbf{non-collusive attack model}, in which all compromised clients share a common adversarial objective but operate independently. Under this model, each attacker generates its malicious update without communicating with other adversaries, accessing other clients' updates, or relying on any knowledge of server-side defenses. To demonstrate the feasibility of this threat model, we propose \textbf{XFED}, the first aggregation-agnostic, non-collusive model poisoning attack. Our empirical evaluation across six benchmark datasets shows that XFED bypasses eight state-of-the-art defenses and outperforms six existing model poisoning attacks. These findings indicate that FL systems are substantially less secure than previously believed and underscore the urgent need for more robust and practical defense mechanisms.

摘要：模型中毒攻擊對聯邦學習（FL）構成了重大安全威脅。大多數現有的模型中毒攻擊依賴於共謀，要求對抗客戶端通過交換本地良性模型和同步生成其中毒更新來協調。然而，在現實世界的 FL 部署中，維持這種協調變得越來越不切實際，因為這實際上需要對許多設備進行類似僵尸網絡的控制。這種方法維護成本高昂，且極易被檢測。這一背景提出了一個根本性問題：在攻擊者之間沒有任何通信的情況下，模型中毒攻擊能否保持有效？為了解決這一挑戰，我們引入並正式化了 \textbf{非共謀攻擊模型}，在這個模型中，所有受損客戶端共享一個共同的對抗目標，但獨立運作。在這個模型下，每個攻擊者在不與其他對手通信、不訪問其他客戶端的更新或不依賴於任何伺服器端防禦知識的情況下生成其惡意更新。為了證明這一威脅模型的可行性，我們提出了 \textbf{XFED}，這是第一個聚合無關的非共謀模型中毒攻擊。我們在六個基準數據集上的實證評估顯示，XFED 繞過了八種最先進的防禦，並超越了六種現有的模型中毒攻擊。這些發現表明，FL 系統的安全性遠低於先前的認知，並強調了對更強大和實用的防禦機制的迫切需求。

##### **Process Reward Agents for Steering Knowledge-Intensive Reasoning**
2604.09482v1 by Jiwoong Sohn, Tomasz Sternal, Kenneth Styppa, Torsten Hoefler, Michael Moor

Reasoning in knowledge-intensive domains remains challenging as intermediate steps are often not locally verifiable: unlike math or code, evaluating step correctness may require synthesizing clues across large external knowledge sources. As a result, subtle errors can propagate through reasoning traces, potentially never to be detected. Prior work has proposed process reward models (PRMs), including retrieval-augmented variants, but these methods operate post hoc, scoring completed trajectories, which prevents their integration into dynamic inference procedures. Here, we introduce Process Reward Agents (PRA), a test-time method for providing domain-grounded, online, step-wise rewards to a frozen policy. In contrast to prior retrieval-augmented PRMs, PRA enables search-based decoding to rank and prune candidate trajectories at every generation step. Experiments on multiple medical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PRA consistently outperforms strong baselines, achieving 80.8% accuracy on MedQA with Qwen3-4B, a new state of the art at the 4B scale. Importantly, PRA generalizes to unseen frozen policy models ranging from 0.5B to 8B parameters, improving their accuracy by up to 25.7% without any policy model updates. More broadly, PRA suggests a paradigm in which frozen reasoners are decoupled from domain-specific reward modules, allowing the deployment of new backbones in complex domains without retraining.

摘要：知識密集型領域的推理仍然具有挑戰性，因為中間步驟往往無法在本地驗證：與數學或程式碼不同，評估步驟的正確性可能需要綜合來自大型外部知識來源的線索。結果，微妙的錯誤可能會在推理過程中傳播，潛在地永遠無法被檢測到。先前的研究提出了過程獎勵模型（PRMs），包括檢索增強變體，但這些方法是在事後運作，對已完成的軌跡進行評分，這阻礙了它們在動態推理程序中的整合。在這裡，我們介紹了過程獎勵代理（PRA），這是一種在測試時提供基於領域的、在線的、逐步獎勵給冷凍策略的方法。與先前的檢索增強PRMs相比，PRA使基於搜索的解碼能夠在每個生成步驟中對候選軌跡進行排名和修剪。在多個醫療推理基準上的實驗表明，PRA始終超越強基線，在MedQA上以Qwen3-4B達到80.8%的準確率，這是4B規模的新最先進技術。重要的是，PRA能夠推廣到未見過的冷凍策略模型，參數範圍從0.5B到8B，將其準確性提高了多達25.7%，而無需任何策略模型更新。更廣泛地說，PRA提出了一種範式，其中冷凍推理器與特定領域的獎勵模塊解耦，允許在複雜領域中部署新的骨幹而無需重新訓練。

##### **E3-TIR: Enhanced Experience Exploitation for Tool-Integrated Reasoning**
2604.09455v1 by Weiyang Guo, Zesheng Shi, Liye Zhao, Jiayuan Ma, Zeen Zhu, Junxian He, Min Zhang, Jing Li

While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated significant potential in Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR), existing training paradigms face significant limitations: Zero-RL suffers from inefficient exploration and mode degradation due to a lack of prior guidance, while SFT-then-RL is limited by high data costs and capability plateaus caused by low-entropy collapse. To address these challenges, we propose E3-TIR (Enhanced Experience Exploitation), a warm-up paradigm for the early stages of agent training. Specifically, we formulate training as the dynamic integration of three experience types: Expert Prefixes, Expert Guided, and Self-Exploration. By executing diverse branching exploration around expert "anchors" and employing a mix policy optimization mechanism, we effectively mitigate distribution shifts and resolve optimization conflicts arising from shared prefixes. Our method dynamically adapts the model's knowledge boundaries, effectively balancing exploration diversity with training efficiency.Experimental results demonstrate that E3-TIR achieves a 6 performance improvement over traditional paradigms on tool-use tasks, while requiring less than 10 of the synthetic data. Furthermore, in terms of ROI, a comprehensive metric integrating performance, data cost, and training efficiency we achieve a 1.46x gain compared to baselines. Code is available at https://github.com/yuki-younai/E3-TIR.

摘要：儘管大型語言模型（LLMs）在工具整合推理（TIR）方面顯示出顯著潛力，但現有的訓練範式面臨重大限制：零強化學習（Zero-RL）因缺乏先前指導而遭受低效探索和模式退化，而先訓練再強化學習（SFT-then-RL）則受到高數據成本和由低熵崩潰引起的能力平台的限制。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了E3-TIR（增強經驗利用），這是一種用於代理訓練早期階段的熱身範式。具體來說，我們將訓練公式化為三種類型經驗的動態整合：專家前綴、專家引導和自我探索。通過在專家“錨點”周圍執行多樣的分支探索並採用混合策略優化機制，我們有效減輕了分佈轉移並解決了由共享前綴引起的優化衝突。我們的方法動態調整模型的知識邊界，有效平衡探索多樣性與訓練效率。實驗結果表明，E3-TIR在工具使用任務上相比傳統範式實現了6的性能提升，同時所需的合成數據少於10。此外，在投資回報率（ROI）方面，綜合性能、數據成本和訓練效率的綜合指標，我們相比基準實現了1.46倍的增益。代碼可在 https://github.com/yuki-younai/E3-TIR 獲得。

##### **UIPress: Bringing Optical Token Compression to UI-to-Code Generation**
2604.09442v1 by Dasen Dai, Shuoqi Li, Ronghao Chen, Huacan Wang, Biao Wu, Qizhen Lan

UI-to-Code generation requires vision-language models (VLMs) to produce thousands of tokens of structured HTML/CSS from a single screenshot, making visual token efficiency critical. Existing compression methods either select tokens at inference time using task-agnostic heuristics, or zero out low-attention features without actually shortening the sequence -- neither truly reduces prefill latency or adapts to the non-uniform information density of UI screenshots. Meanwhile, optical (encoder-side learned) compression has shown strong results for document OCR, yet no prior work has adapted this paradigm to UI-to-Code generation. We propose UIPress, a lightweight learned compression module inserted between the frozen ViT encoder and the LLM decoder of Qwen3-VL-8B. UIPress combines depthwise-separable convolutions, element-guided spatial reweighting, and Transformer refinement to compress ${\sim}$6{,}700 visual tokens to a fixed budget of 256. Together with Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) on the decoder to bridge the representation gap, the entire system adds only ${\sim}$21.7M trainable parameters (0.26\% of the 8B base model). Under a fair comparison on the same base model against four baselines on Design2Code, UIPress at 256 tokens achieves a CLIP score of 0.8127, outperforming the uncompressed baseline by +7.5\% and the strongest inference-time method by +4.6\%, while delivering 9.1$\times$ time-to-first-token speedup. To the best of our knowledge, UIPress is the first encoder-side learned compression method for the UI-to-Code task.

摘要：UI-to-Code 生成需要視覺語言模型 (VLMs) 從單一截圖生成數千個結構化的 HTML/CSS 標記，使得視覺標記效率至關重要。現有的壓縮方法要麼在推理時使用與任務無關的啟發式方法選擇標記，要麼在不實際縮短序列的情況下將低注意力特徵歸零——這兩者都無法真正減少預填延遲或適應 UI 截圖的非均勻信息密度。與此同時，光學（編碼器端學習的）壓縮在文檔 OCR 中顯示出強勁的結果，但之前的研究尚未將這一範式應用於 UI-to-Code 生成。我們提出了 UIPress，一個輕量級的學習壓縮模塊，插入在凍結的 ViT 編碼器和 Qwen3-VL-8B 的 LLM 解碼器之間。UIPress 結合了深度可分離卷積、元素引導的空間重加權和 Transformer 精煉，將約 6,700 個視覺標記壓縮到固定的 256 預算。連同在解碼器上進行低秩適應 (LoRA) 以彌補表示差距，整個系統僅增加約 21.7M 可訓練參數（佔 8B 基礎模型的 0.26\%）。在對同一基礎模型進行公平比較時，對比四個基準，在 Design2Code 上，UIPress 在 256 個標記下達到 0.8127 的 CLIP 分數，超過未壓縮基準 +7.5\% 和最強的推理時方法 +4.6\%，同時提供 9.1$\times$ 的首次標記速度提升。據我們所知，UIPress 是 UI-to-Code 任務中首個編碼器端學習的壓縮方法。

##### **Three Modalities, Two Design Probes, One Prototype, and No Vision: Experience-Based Co-Design of a Multi-modal 3D Data Visualization Tool**
2604.09426v1 by Sanchita S. Kamath, Aziz N Zeidieh, Venkatesh Potluri, Sile O'Modhrain, Kenneth Perry, JooYoung Seo

Three-dimensional (3D) data visualizations, such as surface plots, are vital in STEM fields from biomedical imaging to spectroscopy, yet remain largely inaccessible to blind and low-vision (BLV) people. To address this gap, we conducted an Experience-Based Co-Design with BLV co-designers with expertise in non-visual data representations to create an accessible, multi-modal, web-native visualization tool. Using a multi-phase methodology, our team of five BLV and one non-BLV researcher(s) participated in two iterative sessions, comparing a low-fidelity tactile probe with a high-fidelity digital prototype. This process produced a prototype with empirically grounded features, including reference sonification, stereo and volumetric audio, and configurable buffer aggregation, which our co-designers validated as improving analytic accuracy and learnability. In this study, we target core analytic tasks essential for non-visual 3D data exploration: orientation, landmark and peak finding, comparing local maxima versus global trends, gradient tracing, and identifying occluded or partially hidden features. Our work offers accessibility researchers and developers a co-design protocol for translating tactile knowledge to digital interfaces, concrete design guidance for future systems, and opportunities to extend accessible 3D visualization into embodied data environments.

摘要：三維 (3D) 數據視覺化，例如表面圖，在從生物醫學影像到光譜學的 STEM 領域中至關重要，但對於盲人和低視力 (BLV) 人士來說仍然難以接觸。為了解決這一問題，我們與具有非視覺數據表示專業知識的 BLV 共同設計者進行了基於經驗的共同設計，以創建一個可訪問的、多模態的、網頁原生的視覺化工具。使用多階段的方法論，我們的五名 BLV 和一名非 BLV 研究者團隊參加了兩次迭代會議，將低保真觸覺探針與高保真數位原型進行比較。這一過程產生了一個具有實證基礎特徵的原型，包括參考聲音化、立體和體積音頻以及可配置的緩衝聚合，我們的共同設計者驗證了這些特徵能提高分析準確性和學習能力。在本研究中，我們針對非視覺 3D 數據探索的核心分析任務：定向、地標和峰值查找、比較局部極大值與全局趨勢、梯度追踪，以及識別被遮擋或部分隱藏的特徵。我們的工作為可訪問性研究者和開發者提供了一個共同設計協議，用於將觸覺知識轉換為數位介面，為未來系統提供具體的設計指導，並擴展可訪問的 3D 視覺化至具身數據環境的機會。

##### **Automated Instruction Revision (AIR): A Structured Comparison of Task Adaptation Strategies for LLM**
2604.09418v1 by Solomiia Bilyk, Volodymyr Getmanskyi, Taras Firman

This paper studies Automated Instruction Revision (AIR), a rule-induction-based method for adapting large language models (LLMs) to downstream tasks using limited task-specific examples. We position AIR within the broader landscape of adaptation strategies, including prompt optimization, retrieval-based methods, and fine-tuning. We then compare these approaches across a diverse benchmark suite designed to stress different task requirements, such as knowledge injection, structured extraction, label remapping, and logical reasoning. The paper argues that adaptation performance is strongly task-dependent: no single method dominates across all settings. Across five benchmarks, AIR was strongest or near-best on label-remapping classification, while KNN retrieval performed best on closed-book QA, and fine-tuning dominated structured extraction and event-order reasoning. AIR is most promising when task behavior can be captured by compact, interpretable instruction rules, while retrieval and fine-tuning remain stronger in tasks dominated by source-specific knowledge or dataset-specific annotation regularities.

摘要：這篇論文研究了自動化指令修訂（AIR），這是一種基於規則歸納的方法，用於利用有限的任務特定範例將大型語言模型（LLMs）調整到下游任務。我們將AIR定位於更廣泛的適應策略範疇中，包括提示優化、基於檢索的方法和微調。接著，我們在一個多樣的基準套件中比較這些方法，該套件旨在強調不同的任務需求，例如知識注入、結構化提取、標籤重映射和邏輯推理。論文主張，適應性能與任務密切相關：沒有單一方法在所有設置中都佔優。 在五個基準中，AIR在標籤重映射分類上表現最強或接近最佳，而KNN檢索在閉卷問答中表現最佳，微調則在結構化提取和事件順序推理中佔主導地位。當任務行為可以通過簡潔、可解釋的指令規則捕捉時，AIR最具潛力，而在以源特定知識或數據集特定註釋規律為主的任務中，檢索和微調仍然更強。

##### **Arbitration Failure, Not Perceptual Blindness: How Vision-Language Models Resolve Visual-Linguistic Conflicts**
2604.09364v2 by Farhad Nooralahzadeh, Omid Rohanian, Yi Zhang, Jonathan Fürst, Kurt Stockinger

When a Vision-Language Model (VLM) sees a blue banana and answers "yellow", is the problem of perception or arbitration? We explore the question in ten VLMs with various sizes and reveal an Encoding-Grounding Dissociation: models that fail to report what they see (and thus provide a wrong answer) still encode the visual evidence as strongly as models that provide the correct answer. Using Multimodal Arbitration Crossover (MAC) analysis with layer-by-layer Logit Lens probing, we track the competition between visual and prior signals across every layer of each model. We show that visual attributes can be linearly decodable from early layers (AUC > 0.86). The accuracy remains nearly identical for both successful and failed samples. However, the gap in the final-layer logit - not the strength of encoding - better predicts grounding outcomes with a correlation of $ρ=$ 0.847. After having studied when VLMs base their answers on image clues rather than prior knowledge, we want to understand the causal relationships. We establish causality through full-sequence activation patching. The standard last-token interventions in LLM interpretability do not affect VLMs. In contrast, replacing the full token sequence at layers identified by MAC alters 60 to 84% of outputs. Partial-token decomposition shows that image tokens carry almost all of the causal impact, while text tokens have none. Scaling addresses the remaining architectural differences to achieve perfect retention. Moving from diagnosis to intervention, we show that training-free activation steering - both linear and sparse autoencoder-guided - in early layers can improve visual grounding by up to +3.8% with degrading performance in some setups. Overall, these findings lead to a clear conclusion: VLMs already see well, but the challenge is acting on what they see. Targeted interventions can help to bridge this gap.

摘要：當一個視覺-語言模型（VLM）看到一根藍色香蕉並回答「黃色」，這是感知還是仲裁的問題？我們在十個不同大小的VLM中探討這個問題，並揭示了一種編碼-基礎的分離：那些未能報告所見（因此提供錯誤答案）的模型，仍然像提供正確答案的模型一樣強烈地編碼視覺證據。使用多模態仲裁交叉（MAC）分析，通過逐層的Logit Lens探測，我們追蹤每個模型中視覺信號和先前信號之間的競爭。我們顯示視覺屬性可以從早期層線性可解碼（AUC > 0.86）。成功樣本和失敗樣本的準確性幾乎相同。然而，最終層的logit差距——而不是編碼的強度——更好地預測基礎結果，相關性為$ρ=$ 0.847。在研究VLM何時根據圖像線索而非先前知識來基礎其答案後，我們想了解因果關係。我們通過全序列激活修補建立因果關係。LLM可解釋性的標準最後標記干預對VLM不產生影響。相反，在MAC識別的層中替換整個標記序列會改變60%到84%的輸出。部分標記分解顯示圖像標記幾乎攜帶了所有的因果影響，而文本標記則沒有。擴展解決了剩餘的架構差異，以實現完美的保留。從診斷轉向干預，我們顯示在早期層中無需訓練的激活引導——包括線性和稀疏自編碼器引導——可以將視覺基礎提高多達+3.8%，但在某些設置中性能會下降。總體而言，這些發現得出了一個明確的結論：VLM已經看得很好，但挑戰在於如何對所見做出反應。針對性的干預可以幫助彌補這一差距。
